## PHASE F — POW EXCHANGE CARTEL COLLAPSE — 2026-06-29 (D161, FOCUSED-GATED)
**Prisoner exchange collapse now has a War Effort surface without reopening the cartel or adding a parallel campaign map.** The module teaches the Dix-Hill cartel, the 1863 USCT fault line, camp overcrowding, and relief limits; active relief is visible, capped, and opt-in. Q5 Chattanooga and Q6 USCT playable battles remain LAST.
- **Shipped:** new `data/prisoner-exchange.json` (`cw_prisoner_exchange_v1`) with sourced side profiles, timeline entries, camp notes, debate cards, bridge caps, and capture/mortality rates; new `src/62-prisoner-exchange.js`; manifest registration; War Effort rendering/wiring in `src/20-president-render.js` and `src/30-president-shell.js`; bridge integration in `src/85-battle-bridge.js`; init/resolve registration in `src/90-president-register.js`; and a focused `tools/probe-prisoner-exchange.mjs` included in `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs`. `civil_war_generals.html` was rebuilt from source.
- **Source audit:** existing repo source trails were sufficient, so no web fetch was needed. The data ties the Dix-Hill cartel, Confederate threats against captured Black soldiers, Lincoln's retaliation order, Andersonville, Elmira, and prisoner-camp mortality into one teaching surface. The framing is anti-Lost-Cause and anti-false-equivalence: both sides' camp suffering is named, but cartel collapse is not treated as a neutral accident or an excuse to erase slavery and USCT status.
- **Runtime seam:** the War Effort overview now shows a **Prisoner Exchange & Camps** block with pressure, exchange function, detained burden, mortality risk, side policy, timeline, camp notes, and a **Prioritize relief** toggle. It records detained/returned/died-in-captivity estimates from resolved battle casualties and current cartel stage.
- **Bridge/save:** default inactive POW relief returns exact zero. Only the explicit relief priority can affect the bridge, capped at morale +2, fatigue relief 2, supply cost 2, and overall +1. Active relief mitigates deaths/returns and can add a small transparent returned-prisoner manpower boost; it never reopens the cartel. State rides additive `C.prisoners` with sanitizer/defaults and no `_SAVE_VER` bump.

## PHASE F — STRATEGIC LOGISTICS / RAIL NETWORK — 2026-06-29 (D159)
**Rail and supply now function as strategic arteries of the war without adding a second campaign map.** The milestone is additive and bounded: a War Effort readout teaches the Union railroad/equipment/repair advantage and Confederate fragmentation/iron scarcity/decay, while an opt-in railhead priority can feed small transparent supply/fatigue inputs into the existing battle bridge. Q5 Chattanooga and Q6 USCT playable battles remain LAST.
- **Shipped:** new `data/logistics-rail.json` (`cw_logistics_rail_v1`) with sourced side profiles, theater route notes, campaign benchmarks, debate cards, and bridge caps; new `src/61-logistics-rail.js`; manifest registration; War Effort rendering/wiring in `src/20-president-render.js` and `src/30-president-shell.js`; bridge integration in `src/85-battle-bridge.js`; resolve/init registration in `src/90-president-register.js`; and a focused `tools/probe-logistics-rail.mjs` included in `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs`. `civil_war_generals.html` was rebuilt from source.
- **Source audit:** existing repo source trails were sufficient, so no web fetch was needed. The data follows the economy/history dossier: the U.S. held roughly 22,000 railroad miles and most railroad equipment; the Confederacy had roughly 9,000-9,500 miles, many companies/gauge breaks, weak equipment production, severe iron replacement limits, and declining service. The framing is anti-Lost-Cause: Confederate scarcity is modeled as political economy, slavery-capital conversion limits, fragmented railroads, and material bottlenecks, not as romantic deprivation.
- **Runtime seam:** the War Effort overview now shows a **Rail & Supply Network** block with side-specific strength, repair, depot, bottleneck, and route notes. It does not create a parallel campaign map or new battle.

- **Shipped:** new `data/loot-survival.json`, `src/37-loot-survival.js`, a `Campaign Kit` President-desk tab, and a focused browser probe wired into `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs`. Battle/campaign resolution now recovers deterministic rarity-tiered loot; inventory supports stack caps, unique items, use/equip, and bounded slots.
- **Survival:** rations, exposure, disease, fatigue, forage, and morale live in `C.loot.survival`. Survival pressure is off by default and only reaches the battle bridge through `lootSurvivalBridgeBonus`, which returns exact zero unless survival or a Soldier journey is active.
- **Soldier's Story:** `ssPersonRegistry` reuses the R-5 rating/prosopography substrate to enumerate authored personas, generals/commission figures, and representative company officer/NCO/private rows for every current modeled tactical brigade token. The UI exposes the full current registry for play-as-anyone journey starts (603 selectable people in the current build), while generated rows stay `Inferred` so later citation-grade bios/portraits can replace them honestly.
- **Bug-hunt fix:** stopped registry creation from annotating canonical `GAME_DATA.ratings`, made over-cap stack adds return `stack-full`, preserved explicit zero survival meters on load, and added the full-registry UI selector/probe after finding the first UI only exposed sample cards.
- **Vet:** syntax checks passed for new/edited JS; build **GATE OK**; focused `probe-loot-survival` **8/8, 0 pageerrors**; full no-regression completed green in resumed segments; after the final full-registry UI fix, `npm run vet:noreg -- --from="loot survival"` passed **60 commands**, with `probe-full-campaign` **4/4, 0 pageerrors** and `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`, `m3dActive:false`. JSON readback clean; `git diff --check` clean. Q5 Chattanooga and Q6 USCT playable battles remain LAST.

- **Audit fixes:** do **not** remove probes from the universal scheme. This run proved their value: the new wrapper found a false-red accessibility scan, a `bootprobe` browser-close hang, the `probe-phased-3d` hang, and too-tight heavy-probe budgets. ## PHASE H — H5 increment 4: FORTIFICATIONS DEPTH (the modern engine now digs, holds, bypasses, and commits like UG:G) — 2026-06-26 (D142)
**The 4th and closing step of the locked D138 arc.** This is a **D74 gameplay carve-out**, not byte-identical presentation work: the modern engine now has deeper fortifications, terrain effects wired through the universal sim hooks, and a player charge-impetus commit lock. Hex/Classic remains untouched.
- **Shipped:** `src/tactical/T13-engineering.js` now stages entrenchment from rifle pits / hasty cover to full parapet to redoubt/earthwork, with stage-aware HUD and 2D/3D earthworks. `fldEngCover` is facing-aware: front cover is strongest, flank cover is reduced, and rear bypass still matters; marching off the works removes the live cover while visible works fade. Prepared abatis built from own parapet/redoubt is stronger, slower, clearer, harder to clear, and more punishing to morale/disorder/fatigue.
- **Charge lock + terrain sim hooks:** `src/tactical/T20-order-feel.js` adds the deferred player-only charge lock: 1.2s correction grace, then move/hold/queue/re-aim refuse until contact, target loss, fog loss, own rout, or own death. AI inline charges remain unchanged. `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` wires swamp/town/fort into the universal `fldCoverAt`/`fldMoveFactor` ladder: fort strong cover + assault friction, town hard cover + street friction, swamp soft concealment + major slow; wall/woods/hill behavior remains.
- **Probe updates:** `tools/probe-engineering-corps.mjs` now asserts hasty→parapet→redoubt, facing/bypass behavior, abandoned-cover loss, prepared-abatis bite/clear time, HUD/end-card text, and render hooks. `tools/probe-terrain-readability.mjs` now checks that T22 stays presentation-only while T0 owns the terrain sim effects. `tools/probe-order-feel.mjs` now asserts charge grace, commit blocking, own rout/death release, target-loss release, and no AI queue/dig leakage. `tools/probe-bullrun.mjs` now distinguishes legacy combat terrain from the new universal terrain hooks.
- **Bug-hunt:** direct adversarial audit found one real edge bug: committed charges promised release on own rout/death but `fldChargeLocked` did not test the charging unit's own state. Fixed predicate/HUD and extended the probe (`releasedOnOwnRoutDeath:true`). Other audited surfaces held: one universal model, no per-battle damage fudge, AI charges unchanged, terrain sim reads confined to T0, flank/rear bypass retained, prepared abatis tied to own works.
- **Vet (all GREEN, after the final fix):** `node tools/build.mjs` **GATE OK**; focused probes `probe-engineering-corps` **23/23**, `probe-terrain-readability` **29/29**, `probe-order-feel` **13/13**, `probe-bullrun` **15/15** (all 0 pageerrors); `probe-presets` **26/26**; `probe-phased-ab` **20 comparisons / 0 diffs**; full no-regression battery rerun post-fix **PASSED** (`.tmp/h5-i4-full-noreg-postfix.log`); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `git diff --check` clean. Known tolerated harness noise: `bootprobe ok=true errors=10` without real failure details, and `diag-classic` prints two 404 console lines while still passing the nonblank gate.
- **Cline/DeepSeek cleanup:** restored `HANDOFF.md` after a stale external-agent overwrite falsely claimed `/bin/bash` was missing; current Codex shell/build/probe run proved `/bin/bash` and browser probes work in the live Desktop repo.

## PHASE H — H1 increment 5: PD BATTLE-SCENE IMAGERY ON THE PRE-BATTLE BRIEFING + AARON LOCKED THE UG:G-FIDELITY MODERN-ENGINE DIRECTION — 2026-06-25 (D137 + D138)

- **Coverage (accuracy over completeness):** 6 of 9 marquee battles imaged — bullrun1 (Sudley Ford) · antietam (Gardner Bloody-Lane dead) · fredericksburg (Rappahannock pontoons) · chancellorsville (Russell Marye's-Heights stone-wall dead) · vicksburg (Shirley-House siege lines) · gettysburg (O'Sullivan Harvest-of-Death). 3 IMAGELESS + documented (no clean PD wartime photo): malvern, shiloh, chickamauga.
- **The VIEW discipline caught + rejected 3 non-photographs:** a 1917 birdseye drawn panorama (shiloh), the McElroy/Ohio-Commission battle map (chickamauga), and a book engraving of steamers (shiloh #2) — all failed the genuine-photograph bar. - **Combat byte-identical (D74):** the helper reads only `__ASSETS` + a static `SCENE_IMG` table, never `fldRng`/sim/save; the bridge edit adds ONE guarded call; the briefing is a strategy-layer screen; no combat/T*/data/base/save file touched (git-diff). So the deliverable was never truly portable for photos (the in-game "131 portraits" were the procedural engravings; 155 real PD photos sat unembedded on disk).

## PHASE H ("make it come to life") — BASE-ENGINE FIX: MULTI-PHASE 3D SCENE REBUILD — 2026-06-25 (D132)
The combat-path candidate Aaron chose (AskUserQuestion) over the H1/H2 external-asset layer (deferred — it needs Aaron present for the per-asset IP/licensing review, so it's a poor fit for an unattended run). **Fixes a PRE-EXISTING base bug D131's bug-hunt surfaced** (git-traced to predate T10/H1b): the 4 multi-phase battles (Antietam · Gettysburg · Chickamauga · Vicksburg — recon confirmed every phase declares its own distinct sector terrain + objective) advanced their PHASE in 3D by swapping in a fresh unit cast + fresh terrain + fresh objective, but **never rebuilt the live 3D scene** → new brigades INVISIBLE (no `_u3d` group), the prior phase's unit/officer/supply/arms/eng meshes ORPHANED, and the woods/walls/objective-beacon stranded at the OLD sector. 2D + the headless sim were unaffected → the bug only ever showed in real 3D play of a multi-phase battle.
- **Confirmed empirically FIRST:** the new `tools/probe-phased-3d.mjs` ran against the PRE-FIX build and FAILED decisively (Antietam phase-1 `coverage=0` / `orphans=6`, the objective beacon `dz=65` off the new objective at phase 2) — both symptoms (invisible units AND stale terrain/objective) proven before any code changed.
- **What shipped:** new `fld3dRebuildPhaseScene()` (T0), called from `_fldAdvancePhase` (T8) ONLY when `__FIELD.mode3d` — re-runs the same per-phase build sequence as `fld3dInit` (terrain incl. ground/objective-ring+beacon/walls/markers/woods/water + units + officers/supply/arms/flags/eng), then `_fld3dReaimPhase()` re-frames the survey camera onto the new sector's objective (B-6 side-aware). The scene-level per-phase terrain meshes now route through a `_fld3dTrackPhase` tracker into `__FIELD._phaseScene[]`, disposed by `_fld3dDisposePhaseScene()` at the top of `fld3dBuildTerrain`. Renderer/camera/lights/scene/groups persist; every unit-scoped builder already self-disposes.
- **Architecture — combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** the headless stepper (renderer 'none' → `mode3d` false) NEVER enters the rebuild. No combat/data/save file touched; no `_SAVE_VER`; never `fldRng`. **Proven THREE ways:** `probe-presets` 26/26; a NEW `tools/probe-phased-ab.mjs` headless A/B (4 battles × 5 seeds, committed pre-fix build vs fixed) = **20 comparisons, 0 diffs** (winner/casualties/phase-score/log/steps identical, and historically faithful — Antietam CS-tactical, Gettysburg/Vicksburg US, Chickamauga CS); + all 4 per-battle outcome probes green.
- **Bug-hunt (6 diverse-lens Opus finders → 4 findings, ALL one GPU-leak class, ALL FIXED):** **(HIGH + MED, same)** `fld3dBuildEng` (T13) detached its group without disposing the berm/abatis/pontoon geometries+materials → the Vicksburg siege leaked them every advance → FIXED self-disposing (`_fld3dDisposeGroup` first; they're the group's children); **(MED)** `fld3dBuildWater` (T13) disposed its prior river only AFTER the no-river early-return → a river→no-river advance leaked it → FIXED by moving the dispose above the return; **(LOW)** the T8 catch fully swallowed exceptions, masking the very invisible-brigade failure → FIXED to `console.warn`. A completeness self-check confirmed EVERY builder the rebuild calls now self-disposes (the leak surface is fully closed). (The hunt's automated verify+critic legs were env-blocked — a hung 6th finder + an OOM on the 8 GB Mac during the focused re-run — so they were substituted by inline code-verification of all 4 findings + a standalone completeness-critic agent + the empirical re-vet, the D124/D128 precedent.)

## PHASE H ("make it come to life") — H1b: FLAGS & INSIGNIA DEEPENING — 2026-06-25 (D131)
The H1b increment (`.tmp/phase-h-design.md` item 5; memory `civilwar-idea-brigade-battle-flags`). **`src/tactical/T10-flags.js` already existed** (a basic flag layer) → H1b DEEPENS it (D91 deepen-not-replace). Recon found three real defects in the prior code — the 2D path drew blank rectangles (it computed an SVG + `new Image()` it never drew), corps-badge SHAPES were never rendered (only a text label, and the map was wrong — II=circle, V/VI both "cross"), and badges showed on every battle regardless of date (anachronism) with a roman-numeral substring bug mis-reading "II Corps" as "I Corps". All fixed.
- **What shipped:** (1) **battle-aware flag selection** (`_FLD_BATTLE_META` date/theater/badge table) — First National at Bull Run (the ANV battle flag didn't exist 21 Jul 1861; its creation was prompted by the flag confusion at Manassas) + early West; ANV battle flag mid-war East; Hardee pattern in the native Army of Tennessee; Longstreet's transferred Eastern brigades (Hood/Kershaw/Law) flying the ANV flag even at Chickamauga; (2) **new flag patterns drawn for real** — first-national, hardee (blue + white disc), polk (upright St-George cross, distinct from the ANV saltire), US cavalry guidon; (3) **corrected Kearny-patch corps-badge SHAPES as glyphs** — I=disc, II=trefoil, III=diamond, V=Maltese (cross pattée), VI=Greek cross (distinct), XI=crescent, XII=star — division-coloured (1st=red/2nd=white/3rd=blue) with a light halo for silhouette legibility, ALWAYS paired with a text label (CVD-safe); (4) the **anachronism gate** (badges only at the post-Mar-1863 Eastern fields — Chancellorsville + Gettysburg; earlier fields name the adoption date as a teaching beat); (5) a **working 2D draw** (cached canvas blit, fog-gated) + a deepened **HUD** (flag thumbnail + badge swatch + provenance caption).
- **Architecture — combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. The render fns are reached only via the EXISTING T0 `typeof` seams (probes never call them). Reads sim read-only (`u.name/side/x/z/facing/alive/state`, `__FIELD.scenario/fog/units`) + `G.settings`; writes NO sim field, never `fldRng`, no save-version bump. The install block wraps only `fld3dBuildUnits`/`fld3dDispose` (texture disposal + the reinforcement re-skin) via a generic `_fldFlagKeep` marker-propagation helper. Diff = `src/tactical/T10-flags.js` (deepened) + `tools/probe-flags.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML. No combat/data/save file touched → 9 battles byte-identical (probe-presets 26/26).
- **Citation-grade content (research+verify Workflow, 25 agents: 6 Opus historians × 3-lens default-refute verifiers + synthesis):** the fact-sheet CONFIRMED the core code and added the Chickamauga ANV-transplant split + the Vicksburg Western-flag default, and softened the badge-order citation ("General Orders No. 53" → "Hooker's Circular of 21 March 1863" — the surviving primary doc is a circular; the date is solid). ≥2 reputable sources per flag/badge/date (Encyclopedia Virginia, Smithsonian NMAH, Britannica, confederateflags.org, Tennessee State Museum, crwflags.com FOTW, Washington Times, Gettysburg Flag Works, ABT); anti-Lost-Cause (the battle flag framed factually as a battlefield-recognition device).
- **Accessibility/perf (Intel UHD-617 floor):** flags are STATIC (no motion of their own — only T18's cloth ripple is motion, already reduceMotion-gated), so they render faithfully under reduceMotion. `battleFlags="off"` disables the layer. Cached canvas textures (bounded caches keyed by pattern/colour/size), no per-frame allocation, all flag + corps-badge meshes/textures disposed on rebuild + fldExit. CVD-safe (shape + label, never colour alone); the badge halo keeps the shape legible on any background. The new HUD DOM is WCAG 2.2 AA (every text colour clears 4.5:1 by a wide margin, the img border 3:1, alt text present) — `wcag-auditor` confirmed, no changes.
- **Bug-hunt (6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity · fog-leak · history/Lost-Cause · robustness · perf/GPU · a11y/DOM] × 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 46 agents; critic confidence HIGH).** **1 confirmed finding + 6 critic areas → 3 in-scope fixes + 1 base bug SURFACED + 2 noted:** **(CONFIRMED, MED — a PRE-EXISTING base T0/T8 bug, git-traced to predate T10 → SURFACED, not fixed here)** a phased-battle 3D phase-advance (`_fldBuildPhase`/`_fldAdvancePhase` in the combat-path T8) swaps in new unit ids but never rebuilds the `_u3d` 3D groups → new-phase units get no 3D group + the prior phase's groups orphan; H1b only marginally enlarges the orphaned-mesh footprint (CanvasTextures). Fix belongs in T0/T8 (call `fld3dBuildUnits`+`fld3dBuildFlags` from `_fldAdvancePhase` when `mode3d`) — out of this presentation-only milestone's scope (combat-path / byte-identity risk). **(IN-SCOPE FIXES, applied + re-vetted)** a **reinforcement re-skin** (the `fld3dBuildUnits` wrapper re-runs `fld3dBuildFlags` so reinforcements fly textured flags, not the base plain-colour plane); a **badge silhouette halo** (a dark blue badge was hard to read on the dark HUD); **fog-gate probe coverage** (a fog scene proving no flag/badge betrays a hidden enemy + a static-scan of the 2D guard). **(NOTED for future polish)** batteries fly a brigade flag (artillery used guidons); the US-guidon / CS-cavalry asymmetry. ## PHASE H ("make it come to life") — H4: BATTLE-AMBIENCE AUDIO DEEPENING — 2026-06-25 (D130)
The audio "come-to-life" increment (`.tmp/phase-h-design.md` item 4; D91 "continue audio incrementally"). New `src/tactical/T19-battle-ambience.js` gives the battlefield its voice — a default-OFF, opt-in, stereo-spatialized procedural soundscape bed layered UNDER the existing T9 din+SFX (it DEEPENS T9, does not replace it). Recon first confirmed base.html's `dinSet` already supplies a MONO intensity bed and T9 bridges it — so H4 adds the spatial/located layer the din lacks, pairing 1:1 with the T16 gunsmoke.
- **What shipped:** (1) a continuous **rolling-fire wash** (looping band-passed noise + a swell-LFO tremolo, gain tracking battle intensity — the "one continuous roar"); (2) a **cannonade sub-bass rumble** (looping low-passed brown noise, gated up by the count of brigades actually firing their guns); (3) **located cannon/musket reports** (cannon = sharp crack + body thump + rolling reverberant tail; musket = a filtered-noise volley rip) panned in stereo by the firing brigade's field-x (side-corrected to the camera end) and **fog-gated** (a hidden foe makes no located sound). Discoverable via a new accessible "Battle ambience" On/Off row appended to T9's audio panel; one-time captioned via T9's accessible caption.
- **Architecture — combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. Wraps `fld3dRender`/`fld2dDraw`/`fldExit`/T9's `_fldAudioPanelRows` by ASSIGNMENT, with a generic `keep()` helper that propagates EVERY prior introspection marker (`._atmo`/`._wx`/`._t9audio`/T18's) onto each new wrapper — a marker-chain break the no-regression sweep caught mid-build (probe-atmospherics `ex:false`), fixed before commit. Owns a SEPARATE AudioContext (the AUDIO_SCORE / SOUND one-context-per-subsystem convention). Reads sim firing state read-only; never `fldRng` (audio texture uses `Math.random`, which can't reach the sim seed); no `_SAVE_VER` (the `battleAmbience` flag is lazy-defaulted). The scheduling DECISIONS record in a `FLDAMB` state object regardless of whether a real audio device exists → fully testable headless. Diff = T19 (new) + manifest (T19 after T18) + `tools/probe-audio-ambience.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML.
- **Accessibility/perf (Intel UHD-617 floor):** DEFAULT-OFF (`battleAmbience !== true` → zero sound, never built — the byte-identical-mix default); fully suppressed under `reduceMotion` (the calm default — the T16 convention); volume scaled by the existing `battleLoud` (off→silent) + the master capped low (≤0.20, under the din's 0.26) so it never overwhelms the cues it sits beneath. Located reports defer until the AudioContext is genuinely running (no first-gesture stampede); the bed self-silences on the 'over' screen (no idle-graph drain); the source-voice pool is bounded + all nodes disposed + the context suspended on `fldExit`. CVD-safe; the toggle row reuses T9's AA-vetted segmented-button markup → `wcag-auditor` N/A.
- **Bug-hunt (6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity · webaudio-leaks · fog-leak · edge-robust · a11y-ux · lifecycle] × 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 19 agents; critic confidence HIGH — "NO byte-identity violation, NO fog leak, marker-chain correct").** **1 confirmed + 2 critic-surfaced real edge-bugs + 1 LOW, ALL FIXED:** **(confirmed MED, 3/3)** `fldAmbCaptionOnce` burned the one-shot `captioned` flag BEFORE the caption rendered — but T9's caption no-ops when captions are off (the default), so a user enabling captions mid-battle would never see the cue → the flag is now consumed ONLY inside the captions-on branch; **(critic MED)** the six lenses only saw the probe's always-running context — in the real game it's born SUSPENDED until a gesture, and located reports kept scheduling against the frozen clock → a stacked "stampede" the instant audio resumed → `fldAmbReports` now gates on `ctx.state==="running"`; **(critic LOW)** the live WebAudio graph idled indefinitely on the 'over' screen (master never zeroed there) → `fldAmbUpdate` now silences on `phase==="over"`; **(critic LOW)** StereoPanner nodes shared the source bag, diluting the documented voice cap + a dead `.stop()` per dispose → panners moved to a separate `pans` pool (disconnect-only; the cap counts audible voices). The lifecycle "stale per-phase state" finding was REFUTED 3/3 (singleton `__FIELD`; negative men-delta clamps to 0; cooldowns expire across the interphase card). Probe strengthened 19→22.
- **Vet (all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-audio-ambience` 22/22; `probe-presets` 26/26 (byte-identity, re-confirmed post-fix); `probe-atmospherics` 18/18 (T16 + marker chain) · `probe-weather` 30/30 (T17) · `probe-render-richness` 30/30 (T18) — all coexist; `probe-tactical-visuals` 10/10 (0 tex warnings); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` 14/14. (Audio can't be screenshotted — the probe verifies the WebAudio graph builds + every scheduling decision; the visual-confirmation analog for a sound layer.) Committed + pushed. **NEXT:** H1b flags/insignia → H1/H2 PD imagery (SURFACE first — external assets; an external-audio-file layer is the same kind of fork → SURFACE first). ## PHASE H ("make it come to life") — H3-i3: TERRAIN & UNIT RENDER RICHNESS — 2026-06-24 (D129)
The next Phase-H increment after the weather pass (`.tmp/phase-h-design.md` item 3). New `src/tactical/T18-render-richness.js` makes the battlefield itself feel alive without touching combat.
- **What shipped:** (1) **3D ground vertex-colour enrichment** — procedural grass mottle + dry-ochre / damp-lush / bare-earth patches + tilled crop-row corduroy (positions untouched, colours only); (2) **woods wind-sway** (per-cone tilt-about-base on the InstancedMesh); (3) **banner cloth ripple** (per-unit flag twist/dip); (4) **selection-ring pulse** + a **march bob** for moving brigades; (5) a **casualty fade-out** on death (the brigade settles into the ground + fades). Plus 2D-canvas equivalents (a CACHED soft field-grain, a pulsing selection halo, the same casualty fade).
- **Architecture — combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. Wraps `fld3dBuildTerrain`/`fld3dRender`/`fld3dSyncUnit`/`fld2dDraw`/`fldExit` by ASSIGNMENT (the T9/T16/T17 seam; propagates the `._wx`/`._atmo` markers). All variation is analytic value-noise + wall-clock sines (never `fldRng`); reads only render state + read-only sim fields; writes NO sim field, no `_SAVE_VER`. Ground recolors VERTICES only — units seat on the analytic `fldTerrainH`, never the mesh, so they never float/sink. Byte-identical default: `renderRich="off"` leaves the un-enriched ground + unswayed woods + flat flags. Diff = T18 (new) + manifest + `tools/probe-render-richness.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML.
- **Accessibility/perf (Intel UHD-617 floor):** every MOTION effect is suppressed under `reduceMotion` — the STATIC ground texture stays (faithful detail, not motion; the T17 precedent). `renderRich="off"` disables the layer (motion reverts mid-battle; the ground tint reverts on next launch — the T16/T17 apply-time pattern). Woods sway recomputes from a cached base (no drift); `fldLow()` trims amplitude + grain cells; the **2D field-grain is cached to an offscreen canvas** (built once, blitted with one `drawImage` — no per-frame fillrate on the weakest 2D-fallback GPU). CVD-safe; no new DOM → wcag-auditor N/A.
- **Bug-hunt (6 diverse-lens Opus finders × 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 37 agents; critic confidence HIGH).** **1 substantive bug + 7 real LOWs, ALL FIXED:** **(the one substantive, MED/HIGH across 4 lenses)** the casualty-fade `g.position.y -= (1-rec.fade)*5` was CUMULATIVE (the base never re-seats a dead group's Y) → ~125yd of frame-rate-dependent sink through the terrain → **rewritten ABSOLUTE** off `fldTerrainH`, bounded ~5yd (probe asserts `maxSink ≤ 8`, measured 4.96); pure visual, D74 intact. Plus: a fog-ghost guard (`rec.wasVis` — a fog-hidden enemy that dies no longer pops into view), the selection ring now fades with the corpse, `_rrSetGroupOpacity` no longer flips the T10 flag's transparent flag (alpha-corruption fix), the 2D grain offscreen cache (perf), `renderRich="off"` mid-battle motion revert, a probe sim-field-invariance snapshot (x/z/men/morale/facing), and a counted+once-warned `FLDRR_S.errN` so a swallowed per-unit throw is detectable. Probe strengthened 24→30.
- **Vet (all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-render-richness` 30/30; `probe-presets` 26/26 (byte-identity, re-confirmed post-fix); `probe-atmospherics` 18/18 (T16 coexists); `probe-weather` 30/30 (T17 coexists); `probe-tactical-visuals` 10/10 (0 tex warnings); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` 0 fails. ## PHASE H ("make it come to life") — H3-i2: WEATHER + TIME-OF-DAY ATMOSPHERE — 2026-06-24 (D128)
The natural successor to H3-i1's gunsmoke. New `src/tactical/T17-weather.js` gives each battle a sky and light matched to its real history — re-tinting the 3D background/fog/sun/hemisphere and washing the 2D canvas per a citation-grade per-battle `weather` hint, plus procedural rain/snow precipitation. Design + data-scoping at `.tmp/phase-h-design.md`.
- **What shipped:** sky ∈ clear/overcast/rain/fog/haze/snow × time ∈ dawn/morning/midday/afternoon/dusk → a merged palette applied to the live scene; a second `THREE.Points` cloud (T16 shader pattern) for rain streaks / snow flakes + a faint 2D precip hatch; a one-time accessible weather note via the existing role=status `fldScenarioBanner`. **Marquee visible win: Antietam's pale, warm dawn Cornfield ground-fog** (distant brigades fading into the mist, the objective still readable); the rest carry faithful time-of-day light (warm afternoons, cool mornings).
- **Architecture — combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. Wraps `fld3dInit`/`fld3dRender`/`fld2dDraw`/`fldExit` by ASSIGNMENT (the T9/T16 seam; propagates T16's `._atmo` marker). Reads ONLY the scenario's `weather` hint (`_scenTop.weather` multi-phase, else `scenData.weather`) + render state; OWN LCG (never `fldRng` → sim seed provably unchanged); no sim write, no `_SAVE_VER`. **Byte-identical default:** a missing hint, or `clear`/`midday`, resolves to `null` → ZERO change (every shipped look preserved). Diff = T17 (new) + manifest + 9 `data/*.json` weather blocks + `tools/probe-weather.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML.
- **Citation-grade data (research+verify Workflow, 18 agents: 9 Opus historians × 9 default-refute verifiers):** the verifiers REFUSED to fabricate drama — Gettysburg `haze→clear` (Rev. Jacobs' instrument log: bright at the 2pm Pickett's-Charge window), Fredericksburg `fog→clear/afternoon` (the Rappahannock fog lifted ~10am, before the assault — the note still teaches it), Shiloh `clear/morning` (the rain was OVERNIGHT), and a misattributed Vicksburg source removed. **The honest finding: the "fog of war" at most of these battles was POWDER-SMOKE (T16), not weather** — only Antietam's dawn fog is a real non-clear sky. ≥2 sources each, anti-Lost-Cause.
- **Accessibility/perf (Intel UHD-617 floor):** the static tint is motion-free → applies under `reduceMotion`; only PRECIPITATION is suppressed under it (tint kept — probe-verified). `weather="off"` disables the layer. Fog far-plane held ≥1500 in every palette so the objective never vanishes. One precip draw call + `fldLow()` budget (520/200) + a `gl_PointSize` driver clamp. CVD-safe; no new DOM → wcag-auditor N/A (the note reuses the AA-vetted banner).
- **Decided-&-logged (D61):** Antietam's dawn-fog applies to all 3 phases (it opened the Cornfield, thinned later) — kept as the iconic battle signature; per-phase weather logged as a future H3-i3 add (the bug-hunt verifiers split on it → simplification, not defect).
- **Bug-hunt (6 diverse-lens Opus finders × 3-skeptic default-refute + a critic; the critic leg STALLED, substituted by an inline completeness pass — the D124 precedent).** 8 findings; **1 HIGH fixed:** the atmosphere note re-fired EVERY frame (`_wxLaunchKey` keyed on `__FIELD.seed`, which `fldRng` mutates each tick) → re-keyed on the stable `__FIELD.scenario` + a note-once probe assertion. **1 LOW (real) fixed:** inherited-property sky names (`constructor`/`__proto__`) bypassed the `!FLDWX.SKY[sky]` guard → `hasOwnProperty` validation + a malformed-input assertion. Precip-dispose + malformed-input locked by new assertions; the `fld3dDispose`-wrap finding refuted 3/3. A probe test-pollution bug (synth scenes mutated the shared `GAME_DATA` weather object) was caught by the note-once assertion + fixed (shallow-copy inject).
- **Vet (all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-weather` 30/30 (byte-identical default · each palette applies · fog far ≥1500 on the real fog battle · `wxPrecip` built + DISPOSED · reduceMotion suppresses precip keeps tint · once-per-launch note · malformed safety · `gl_PointSize` clamp · sim seed UNCHANGED across the wx loop); `probe-presets` 26/26 (byte-identity → combat byte-identical); `probe-atmospherics` 18/18 (T16+T17 coexist, transitive marker); `probe-tactical-visuals` 10/10 (tinted battles render, beacons seated, 0 tex warnings); `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `t1probe` ok; broad no-regression GREEN in isolation (a batched sweep threw spurious `steps:0` launch failures from 8 GB-Mac memory pressure under concurrent sweep+bug-hunt; isolation re-runs all GREEN). Light-menu-safe (`.gn-paper` uses neither token); HC mode re-redefines both at higher specificity. Authored by me + 4 disjoint-file Sonnet editors.

## RATING SYSTEM — Q12: THE DIVISION SUB-TIER — seat pool generals into division billets nested under each seated corps (the next rung of the GM depth-chart) — 2026-06-23 (D110 — Codex code + Claude vetting/doc close-out)

A division was a **Maj. Gen.'s** billet in BOTH armies (distinct from the corps tier's side-aware grade), so any Brig. Gen. seated over a division leads `belowGrade` until promoted (the Q9 synergy). **Byte-identical until a division is seated** (lift 0; a vacant division = 0, NOT a penalty; pre-Q12 saves with no record read identically via the `_cmdDivLift` fast-path). One billet per man; vacating a corps CASCADES (orphaned divisions stop contributing lift at the READ layer `cmdDivSeated`/`_cmdDivLift`, `_cmdDivClean`:795); `cmdInit` sanitizes on load; no `_SAVE_VER` bump; NO RNG. `data/ratings.json` `divisionCommand` (Inferred + 2 sources: Glatthaar, Weigley).

## RATING SYSTEM — Q8b: THE BETWEEN-BATTLE CAVALRY RECONNAISSANCE ("scout the enemy") — tier-reveal the enemy OOB, scaled by the appointed general's cavalry — 2026-06-23 (D107)

Intel is fresh per engagement (the scout record is keyed to the next-battle id → reverts to light when the battle changes).

EARNED → +confidence rep; ABOVE merit → ×1.8 capital + a jealousy rep HIT — so over-promoting a favorite can LOWER his OVR (rank ≠ competence; anti-Lost-Cause). ## RATING SYSTEM — R-3: the badge engine (the first rating→combat seam) + the no-fudge build-gate — 2026-06-22 (D97)
The first place a rating TOUCHES combat. A guarded one-token factor seeds the levers the engine already reads; the no-fudge OUTPUT wall is now enforced by the build. **Byte-identical when off** — proven across sandbox + all 9 battles (R-3 build vs committed R-2, identical deterministic results).
- **`fldBadgeFactor(u,lever)`** (T14) — guarded multiplicative factor, IDENTITY 1.0 when badges off / no matching badge; sums the unit's badge `mag`s for a lever, gates by trigger, clamps the sum to the realism-scaled per-lever cap (arcade .16 / balanced .10 / historian .06). Negatives are dampers (≥1−cap), never enemy buffs. Plus `fldUnitCohesion` (rally term, 0 when unauthored → byte-identical).
- **Four guarded seams** (T0): fire (fldResolveFire), rally+cohesion (fldMoraleStep), melee (fldResolveMelee), speed (fldMoveFactor). `__FIELD.badges` gate (default ON, `_badgesOff` hook) + `__FIELD.realismTier` (T6 fldPresetsApply).
- **Badge data** (data/ratings.json): 25 badgeDefs gain `fldLever` + signed `mag`. Ships Star/Superstar positives + the Verified negatives with bite (McClellan Slows / Bragg Piecemeal / Burnside Rigid / Green Levies / Powder-Shy). NOT yet assigned to shipped rosters (that's R-6) → battles byte-identical.
- **No-fudge OUTPUT-WALL build-gate** (build.mjs gate 4d): scans the rating module for any cas/aCas/bCas/.victory/.men/sev.* write (dot AND bracket notation), build FAILS (exit 5) if found. Verified firing on planted `u.men=0`, `u["men"]=0`, `F.sev["attrition"]=2`; clean build prints `GATE OK · … · no-fudge ✓`.
- **Vetting — ENVIRONMENTAL DEVIATION:** the standard `load`-based probe suite was blocked this session (headless-Chrome `load` never fires for the game page — the THREE-CDN script stalls in headless; broke the committed R-2 build identically; trivial page loads in 73ms; domcontentloaded loads everything). Contributors: single-threaded `python http.server` chokes on the page's ~170 asset requests (use ThreadingHTTPServer), + the THREE-CDN `load` stall. ## CHICKAMAUGA (Phase C-2 Western breadth) — the river of death, a 3-phase epic (the woods → Longstreet's breakthrough → Thomas at Snodgrass Hill) — 2026-06-21
- **What it is:** the bloodiest battle of the Western theater, built as a 3-phase battle on the T8 multi-phase engine: **P0 The Battle in the Woods (Sep 19)** → **P1 Longstreet's Breakthrough (Sep 20, the Brotherton gap)** → **P2 The Rock of Chickamauga (Sep 20 afternoon, Thomas holds Snodgrass Hill / Horseshoe Ridge)**. New `data/chickamauga.json` + one registry line in `src/tactical/T1-bull-run.js` (menu rank 60, after Vicksburg) + `tools/probe-chickamauga.mjs` + `tools/sweep-chickamauga.mjs`. The teaching is **CONTINGENCY OVER GENIUS** (the breakthrough was handed to Longstreet by the Wood gap order, not Confederate martial superiority) and **the squandered victory** (Bragg failed to pursue → the siege of Chattanooga → the November reversal). Universal gun-count model only; **no per-battle damage fudge** (D74).
- **Framing decision (decide-&-log, no fork surfaced):** Chickamauga + Chattanooga = the C2 "Chickamauga/Chattanooga" item built as a matched PAIR of separate 3-phase epics (the Antietam/Gettysburg precedent), each its own vetted milestone; this milestone = Chickamauga, next = Chattanooga. **Top-level `attacker: CS` / `defender: US` across all 3 phases** — the Army of the Cumberland fought on the defensive throughout, so the CS player takes the offensive (Bragg/Longstreet) and the US player holds (Thomas); cleaner than Vicksburg's US-attacker-throughout and sets up Chattanooga as the US-offensive MIRROR.
- **Research+verify (Workflow, Sonnet finders × Opus adversarial verify + synthesis):** corrected real errors before authoring — **Hood wounded Sep 20 / Maj. Gen.** (not Sep 19 / Lt. Gen.), **Helm in Breckinridge's division** (not Cleburne's), **Cheatham restored** to the OOB, **Granger & W.H.T. Walker = Maj. Gen.** (not Brigadier), **Loring removed** (not at Chickamauga), the gap-reporter left flagged (Kellogg vs Bond disputed), and the **"River of Death"** Cherokee gloss shipped only as disputed folk etymology, never as fact.
- **Balance (AI-vs-AI, 32 seeds, deterministic — the D74 principle; outcomes from OOB/terrain/timing/weight, NO fudge):** P0 woods US-holds 32/32 (mutual bloodbath ~2,400 each — "nobody could see enough to win"; the Union line held Sep 19, historical); P1 Brotherton breakthrough **CS 32/32** (the US routed cheaply, US:CS ~5.1; scoreWeight **3** — the decisive phase); P2 the Rock **US-holds 32/32** with the CS assault paying **CS:US ~3.0** (the failed-assault lesson, mirrored from Fredericksburg). **Aggregate CS 32/32** (CS 3 / US 2 via the weight-3 breakthrough) — a clear Confederate tactical victory in which Thomas's stand prevents annihilation; and a human US player who closes the gap in P1 OVERTURNS the battle (the Wood-gap alt-history hinge). The CS, who won the field, **bled MORE in aggregate** (~70k vs ~63k over 8 seeds) — the costly-victory teaching, now probe-guarded.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (Workflow, 10 Opus agents — 6 diverse-lens finders × default-refute verify + a completeness critic): 2 confirmed + 3 critic gaps, ALL fixed.** HIGH (critic, the Vicksburg-class defect): **Charles Harker mis-ranked "Brig. Gen." under a Verified stamp — he was a COLONEL at Chickamauga** (like Hans Heg, whom the data gets right; his brigadier-generalcy was dated to the battle but came afterward) → corrected to **Col. Charles Harker** + a fact-check probe guard. Plus 4 probe-rigor guards added: the P1 breakthrough casualty-direction (US routed cheaply, US:CS ≥2.5), the P0 winner gate (the line holds ≥7/8), the P1 win-by-SEIZE check (winBy "hold", not a degenerate destroy/timeout), and the aggregate "the winner bled more" guard (CS aggregate casualties > US).
- **Verification (PROPER VETTING):** build GATE OK; `probe-chickamauga` **18/18**, 0 pe (with the tightened guards); full no-regression GREEN — bullrun 15 · malvern 24 · antietam 16 · fredericksburg 22 · chancellorsville 24 · gettysburg 16 · shiloh 29 · vicksburg 18 · roster 8 · field 13 · officers 15 · logistics 14 · arms 23 · presets 26 · csplayer 16 · campaign-link 16 · fog 13 · ai 15 · autopause 13 · custom-builder 9 (its EXPECTED registry baseline updated to include `chickamauga` — the recurring D86/D88 gotcha) · engineering-corps 22 · tactical-visuals (now 10 scenes incl. live Chickamauga 2D/3D, textureWarnings:0); diag-classic nonBlank 346; boot/t1 ok; **0 pageerrors**. ## ENGINEERING CORPS (Phase F) — increment 3: PONTOON BRIDGING (the pontoon train) → CORPS COMPLETE — 2026-06-21
- **What it is:** the third and last increment of "all of the above" — the Engineering Corps is now complete (entrench D87 · abatis D88 · pontoons D89). An OPT-IN river (`__FIELD.terrain.rivers[]`) gates movement: impassable except at a crossing — a shallow ford (slow + fatiguing), a deep ford (fordable only at Arcade; needs a bridge at Balanced/Historian), or a player-laid pontoon bridge (key **N** / "Pontoon"): an infantry pioneer detail on the near bank lays a bridge over realism-scaled time → opens a fast corridor. Surfaced via Skirmish → Ground → "River crossing" (+ `opts.river` for the probe).
- **B-5 coupling:** `fldEngRealism()` scales sapper/pontoon build speed, ford slow, AND deep-ford fordability (`DEEP_FORD_CAP` 0.85). The strategic Engineer Works Corps (`bridgeArmy.engineering`) → `__FIELD.engCorpsSpeed` (set in T2 `fldCampaignCondition`) lays bridges faster on a campaign launch (A1 anchor); standalone stays 1 (byte-identical).
- **Byte-identical / player-only:** the active gate reuses the T0 seams reserved for it (`fldEngMoveFactor` ford slow + `fldEngMoveGate` bank clamp); no shipped scenario declares `terrain.rivers` and the AI never lays a pontoon, so every AI-vs-AI baseline is byte-for-byte unchanged (reads gated by `rv && rv.length` / `engPontoons`; reset per-launch + per-phase). One T0 seam edit: `fldStepMovement` settles a no-progress river clamp to HOLD (the soft-deadlock fix), `eg`-gated → riverless identical. 2D water+boats / 3D water plane+pontoon (leak-managed, fog/low-tier aware); citation-grade Fredericksburg/James-River teaching card (research+verify workflow, 30/38 claims survived adversarial verification).
- **DECISIONS (decide-&-log):** Bull Run's creek/Stone Bridge stay cosmetic (live would regress a shipped battle); AI river-pathing/AI-built works is the named extension point (player-tool this increment), so a river skirmish frames the PLAYER as the attacker (river placed between the player's home edge and the objective, either side) while the AI defends the far bank.
- **Bug-hunt (19 agents, Opus): 8 confirmed + 6 critic, all fixed** — the open-ford→deep-water sidestep leak (+ midpoint sample for tangential bends), the buried 3D water plane (raised to a thin on-ground sheet, fords lifted), the march-in-place soft-deadlock at the bank (settle to HOLD), the degenerate CS-player river framing (placed by player side), a silent crossing-refusal (aria-live + HUD halt line), dupe-span message, pontoon `side` + per-side cap.

## CUSTOM BATTLE BUILDER C4 — single-phase scenario authoring tool — 2026-06-18
- **What it is:** Codex added a first-class **Custom Battle Builder** main-menu flow for the real-time `__FIELD` tactical engine. It is a real builder surface, not a landing page: author scenario name/date/place, field size, objective, sides/briefs, terrain hills/woods/walls/markers, OOB units, artillery/guns, reinforcement timing, optional leaders, supply trains, teaching cards, and provenance.
- **Implementation:** new `src/tactical/T11-custom-battle.js` plus a manifest entry. Custom scenarios stay out of `fldScenarioRegistry()` so the historical roster remains exact; `fldScenarioData(id)` now falls back to `fldCustomScenarioData(id)` only for explicit `custom_...` IDs. Valid custom scenarios launch through the existing single-phase `fldScenarioInit` path, using the same `oob`, `reinforcements`, `terrain`, `objective`, leaders, supply, and universal gun-count artillery model as historical battles. `FLD.BASE_FIELD_W/H` reset field size every launch, while single-phase scenario data may safely set `field.w/h`.
- **Schema/validation:** C4 is intentionally **single-phase V1**. Phase authoring is deferred until a phase editor can be probed as safely as authored `phases[]` data. Validation blocks missing required metadata, unsafe IDs/prototype keys, duplicate IDs, objective overflow, out-of-bounds/clamped numerics, invalid reinforcement timing, side ownership mistakes, unrealistic artillery crew ratios (12-40 crew per gun), malformed JSON, `phases[]`, and forbidden battle-specific combat/damage keys. There are no per-custom-battle damage fudges.
- **Import/export/persistence:** export produces shareable JSON (`{schema:"cw_custom_battle_v1", scenario:{...}}`); import round-trips canonical scenario data and rejects malformed/unsafe JSON without page errors. Six local persistence slots live in `localStorage` under `cw_custom_battles_v1`; saved scenarios are discoverable only by explicit custom ID and can be launched through the field path.
- **Focused probe:** new `tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` verifies builder render, validation failures, valid scenario creation, export/import round trip, UI malformed-import rejection, slot save/list/load/delete, explicit custom-ID launch contract, shared gun model, field-size reset, no phase leak, no Classic `G.battle`, and no historical registry contamination. Current result: **9/9 steps ok, 0 fail**; JSON/screenshot artifacts in `tools/shots/probe-custom-battle-builder.*`.
- **Verification:** `node tools/build.mjs` GATE OK; `node tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` 9/9; `node tools/probe-tactical-roster.mjs` 8/8; `node tools/probe-field.mjs` 13/13; `node tools/probe-bullrun.mjs` 15/15; `node tools/probe-malvern-hill.mjs` 24/24; `node tools/probe-antietam.mjs` 16/16; `node tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs` 22/22; `node tools/probe-chancellorsville.mjs` 24/24; `node tools/probe-gettysburg.mjs` 16/16; `node tools/probe-shiloh.mjs` 29/29; `node tools/probe-officers.mjs` 15/15; `node tools/probe-logistics.mjs` 14/14; `node tools/probe-arms.mjs` 23/23; `node tools/probe-presets.mjs` 26/26; `node tools/probe-csplayer.mjs` 16/16; `node tools/probe-campaign-link.mjs` 16/16; `node tools/probe-tactical-visuals.mjs` 6/6; `node tools/bootprobe.mjs` ok=true with known/tolerated 404 resource console entries and no real errors; `node tools/t1probe.mjs` ok=true; `node tools/diag-classic.mjs` Classic paints (`nonBlank:346`, only pre-existing 404 resource messages); `git diff --check` clean.
- **Next:** C4 is complete. Continue Phase C breadth with Western theater work (Vicksburg / Chickamauga-Chattanooga / Atlanta-March / Franklin-Nashville), C3 USCT battles, or the next Codex-owned roadmap item.

## MALVERN HILL — Phase C-1 Eastern marquee battle (Seven Days artillery duel) — 2026-06-18
- **What it is:** Codex added the remaining Eastern marquee battle as a data-driven single-phase scenario: Malvern Hill, July 1, 1862, the Seven Days' culminating artillery duel. It models Lee's failed, poorly coordinated Confederate assault against Fitz John Porter's Union line and Henry Hunt's massed artillery on the open Malvern plateau. The scenario is CS attacker / US defender, fog off by default, and uses the established cautious-assault pattern to represent piecemeal attacks without touching combat math.
- **Implementation:** new `data/malvern-hill.json` with historical menu/side-choice/brief/end-note text, leaders/fates, terrain (Malvern Hill plateau, Crew House ridge, open killing fields, approach woods/ravines, roads, James River gunboat marker), OOB, reinforcements, teaching cards, and codex entry. `src/tactical/T1-bull-run.js` registers `malvernHill` from `GAME_DATA["malvern-hill"].malvernHill` and orders the public roster First Bull Run → Malvern Hill → Antietam → Fredericksburg → Chancellorsville → Gettysburg → Shiloh. Help copy now names the new battle.
- **Probe:** new `tools/probe-malvern-hill.mjs` verifies data/historical guardrails, single-phase launch, cautious CS attacker, terrain cover, no wall-pattern import, universal gun-count artillery (US 50 guns vs CS 22 in the scenario abstraction), no battle-specific damage/fudge keys, reinforcement timing/idempotency, deterministic AI-vs-AI resolution, US-defender-favored 8-seed balance, passive US/CS player launches, side-aware objective/end-note framing, menu/side-card rendering, and light roster regressions. `tools/probe-tactical-roster.mjs` now guards seven historical battles and the updated order.
- **Balance result:** `probe-malvern-hill` reports seed 101 as US timeout at 500s, US losses 1,336, CS losses 6,545; 8-seed balance US 7/8, CS 1/8. That gives the intended historical shape: the gun line usually holds, but a better-coordinated Confederate attack can overturn history.

## CHANCELLORSVILLE — Phase C-1 Eastern marquee battle (Jackson's flank march) — 2026-06-18
- **What it is:** The third Eastern marquee battle for the __FIELD real-time engine — Lee's greatest victory and his costliest. Outnumbered ~2:1 (133,000 US vs 60,000 CS), Lee splits his army and sends Jackson on a twelve-mile flank march through the tangled Wilderness to crush Hooker's unsuspecting XI Corps. The battle is modeled as a SINGLE-PHASE engagement (the Fredericksburg/Shiloh pattern) focused on the decisive action: Jackson's flank attack on the Union right, with the Confederate assault pressing toward the Chancellor House and the Union defense trying to rally and hold the crossroads.
- **Implementation:** `data/chancellorsville.json` — citation-grade, anti-Lost-Cause, with full OOB (5 US brigades + 1 battery, 4 CS brigades + 1 battery + cavalry), 4 leaders per side with historical fate (Jackson fate=0.12 — mortally wounded by friendly fire; Paxton fate=0.3 — killed; Hooker fate=2.2 — concussed but survived; Berry fate=0.35 — killed), 3 reinforcement waves (Sedgwick's VI Corps, Anderson's Division, Whipple's Division), terrain (the Wilderness woods, Chancellor House ridge, Hazel Grove, Fairview, breastworks, roads), 5 teaching cards (the flank march, Hooker's lost nerve, Jackson's death, the cost of victory, the XI Corps scapegoats), and a codex entry. Registered in `src/tactical/T1-bull-run.js` (registry + menu rank 35 between Fredericksburg and Gettysburg). ## UNIVERSAL AI IMPLEMENTER STANDARDS — 2026-06-18 — same contract for Codex, Cline, DeepSeek, and VS Code agents
- **What it is:** Aaron asked that any model implementing instructions through VS Code follow the same standards and instructions, including recursive self-learning/self-auditing best practices.
- **Docs updated:** `START-HERE.md` now has a Universal AI implementer standards section. `AUTONOMOUS-RUN.md` §1A makes it standing operating law. `HANDOFF.md` and `WAKE-UP.md` point incoming agents at the contract, and the remaining-work/model-routing prompt now requires self-audit checklists, stop conditions, and recursive repo-learning notes.
- **Standard defined:** repo-ground first; work in small reversible edits; preserve unrelated changes; verify with build/probes/JSON/screenshots instead of assumption; self-audit the diff against the user request; fix root causes rather than weakening probes; keep history/assets/licensing honest; report files, commands, results, residual risks, and unverified areas.
- **Recursive self-learning definition:** models learn only through repo-visible artifacts: decisions, run-log entries, handoff updates, checklist notes, and stronger probes. No hidden memory is treated as project truth.
- **Model routing:** Codex/high-reasoning owns architecture, simulation, balance, probes, bug hunts, WCAG judgment, cross-module integration, and final review. Cline/DeepSeek/lower models only execute bounded packets with exact files, steps, constraints, acceptance criteria, commands, expected outputs, rollback, and do-not-touch lists; they must stop on ambiguity or any red gate.

## PHASE C-1.5 · THE UNIVERSAL ARTILLERY GUN MODEL — D75 SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED (2026-06-16) — the FIRST Antietam sub-milestone
- **What it is:** the D74 "universal-combat" cleanup (do FIRST): replace Fredericksburg's per-battle artillery **volume-of-fire proxy men** fudge (C-1/D73 inflated battery `men` to 500/440/500) with a CONSISTENT gun-count model used identically in EVERY battle. Shipped + pushed as its own vetted unit before Antietam. ≈**1749.6KB**.
- **The model (T5):** `FLDA.GUN_FIRE_WEIGHT`=27 (men-equivalent per gun, UNIVERSAL); `fldArtFireStr(u)` → a gun battery fires `guns*27*clamp(men/maxMen)` (rated fire from the gun count, crew-scaled), infantry / arms-off / a legacy no-`guns` battery → `u.men` exactly as before. Wired at `fldResolveFire`'s `strF` (T0); `guns` carried data→unit via `fldMakeUnit` (T0) + `fldBrSpec` (T1). Calibrated so a 6-gun battery ≈ Bull Run's realistic 160-men/6-gun batteries → the model REPRODUCES them (consistent, not just gated). Gun count = army-size-invariant hardware (strength flows through the Cannon-Corps `_canisterScale`, documented).
- **Byte-identity:** only a battery declaring `guns` takes the new path; every baseline has none → byte-identical. field 13 · bullrun 15 · fog 13 · autopause 13 · ai 15 · campaign-link 16 · officers 15 · logistics 14 · presets 26 · csplayer 16 · **arms 23** — all byte-identical, 0 pe; boot ok; t1 14; diag-classic **346**.

RE-VET: **CS 8/8**, casualty ratio **2.06:1** (better than the proxy's 1.91), the stone wall measurably **load-bearing** (cuts CS loss 18-23%, 5/5 CS wins), the crest guns **survive 8/8** + fire — **probe-fredericksburg 22/22, 0 pe**.
- **Bug-hunt (22 agents, 6 finders × 3-skeptic default-refute + a critic):** **0 confirmed finder bugs** (all 5 refuted — the change is correct) + **5 completeness-critic gaps ALL FIXED:** the probe's `u.men0` typo → `maxMen`; a new crest-guns-survive+fire guard; a half-crew crew-scaling assertion; + documented the campaign-strengthMul semantics + the legacy-HUD migration boundary. Also rewrote the wall-load-bearing probe from a noisy single-seed test into a robust multi-seed CS-casualty-reduction test. WCAG clean (gun-count HUD 15.79:1).

## PHASE C-1 · FREDERICKSBURG (Marye's Heights) — D73 SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED (2026-06-16) — PHASE C BEGINS
- **What it is:** the SECOND data-driven tactical battle on the now-mature engine (Eastern marquee first, D69). Burnside's army storms the open glacis toward the sunken Telegraph Road; Longstreet holds the 4-foot stone wall under the pre-sighted Marye's Heights guns. New `data/fredericksburg.json` + `tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs` + the T1/T7 data-driven scenario-UI generalization + a small gated T0 engine seam. ≈**1743.6KB**.
- **The reusable spine:** the engine is now battle-AGNOSTIC — `fldScenarioRegistry()`/`fldScenarioData(id)` (T1) map any registered id → its `GAME_DATA.<battle>` object, and `fldScenarioInit` builds it from the SAME shape. Adding a battle = a data file + a registry line, NO new combat code (Bull Run resolves byte-identical).
- **Data-driven UI (T1+T7):** `fldInjectScenarioButtons` iterates the registry (Bull Run keeps its bespoke marquee button; others build from `data.menu`) + returns the last button to anchor the skirmish/preset buttons; `fldLaunchBattle` fires the briefing for ANY scenario; `fldScenarioSideChoice(id,go)` reads `sd.sides` (a per-battle side-choice card); `fldBriefObjectiveHtml` keeps the keyword skeleton + a data flavor (`sd.brief`); `fldScenarioEndHtml` keeps the Bull Run branch byte-identical (shared `_fldScenarioEndBox`) + a data `sd.endNote` branch. `bullrun.json` gained inert `sides`/`brief` (reproduces its exact copy from data).
- **The doomed-frontal-assault posture (gated T0 seam):** the B-1 attacker is *competent* (column-rush + mass bayonet), which Fredericksburg's assault was NOT. `data.assaultDoctrine:"cautious"` → `__FIELD._atkCautious` makes the AI attacker advance IN LINE and trade but never column-rush nor carry the wall (Burnside's piecemeal disaster). `var aggressive = !__FIELD.fog && !__FIELD._atkCautious` gates the assault/column branches → **default off → byte-identical Bull Run/sandbox/skirmish (ai 15/15, field 13/13).** A HUMAN Union player is unbound (the alt-history hook).
- **Not a fog default (no fog-teaching contradiction):** Bull Run defaults fog ON (D67); Fredericksburg keeps fog OFF (the morning fog had LIFTED — clear fields of fire) and wins the defense by the cautious posture + the stone wall (1.7 cover) + massed crest canister. Two complementary, battle-faithful levers.
- **Bug-hunt caught the balance's core flaw (a real HIGH, fixed pre-commit):** 5 diverse-lens Opus finders × default-refute verify + a completeness critic → **4 confirmed + 5 critic gaps.** The HIGH (empirically traced): `fldAiDefender` holds the objective's FORWARD FACE (`obj.z+obj.r*0.55`); my first geometry put that forward of the wall → the AI marched the line OFF the wall into the open on tick 1, so the 1.7 cover was never used (static-terrain probe missed it). **Fix (the Bull Run pattern):** `obj.z` 375→331 so the forward face lands ON the wall in cover, + `ATK_CAUTIOUS_HOLD` 0.6→0.85 so the cautious attacker holds in the OPEN just outside the wall's cover band (only the attacker exposed). Added a LIVE cover assertion (defenders REMAIN at the wall ≥1.5; attacker hold line exposed). Also fixed the side-card aria role hardwired US=attack → threaded the data `attacking` flag. Gaps: human win requires clearing the position incl. rear guns (objective note reworded); `endNote.draw` now probe-asserted. ACCEPTED-as-intentional: the generic objective skeleton reworded Bull Run's CS line (keywords + flavor preserved; the directive authorized neutralizing Bull-Run-specific copy).

## PHASE B-3 · IN-BATTLE LOGISTICS — D66 SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED
- **What it is:** an ammunition economy on the real-time field. New `src/tactical/T4-logistics.js` + guarded T0 seams + the Bull Run `supply` block + `tools/probe-logistics.mjs`. Each side fields a rear ammunition train w/ a finite reserve; a disengaged brigade within reach refills (draining it); a brigade out of cartridges on the objective fires dry → bayonet (the 20th Maine); a SPENT brigade (fatigue>84) drags. Attacker train far behind its start (outruns its supply), defender train just behind the objective. Ties strategic supply (reserve ∝ `bridgeArmy().supply`; a raid cuts the enemy's). Gated + byte-identical behind `__FIELD.logistics`. ≈1608KB.
- **The fog inversion (the headline):** the 64-agent bug-hunt found that with FOG ON, logistics INVERTED "fog aids the defender" (D58/D64) — Bull Run AI-vs-AI fog-ON CS 8/8 → 0/8 (the attacker cycled fresh brigades to its safe far-rear train and out-sustained the long fog fire-trade). **Surfaced to Aaron** (contradicts a shipped teaching + fork #2). His first pick (a defender's-depot rule) provably did nothing — the defender wasn't the ammo-bottlenecked side; the only lever that works (Aaron-approved) is **choking the ATTACKER's resupply under fog** (`ATK_FOG_RESUPPLY`=0 — an attacker advancing blind can't run its trains forward; a sharp threshold, even 0.15 fails). Result: logistics is balance-NEUTRAL in BOTH fog states (fog-OFF CS 5/8, fog-ON CS 8/8). A FOG REGRESSION GUARD probe step locks it. Also kept the fog-gated scan (AI ignores hidden enemies).
- **Bug-hunt:** 64 agents → 9 confirmed + 2 critic gaps, ALL ADDRESSED (1 HIGH fog + 6 LOW probe-fidelity/correctness: probe boundary test at 240, two-sided balance band, untested asymmetry + fog-reveal + supply-curve probe steps, reinforcement-only-side train). Two refuted findings re-evaluated (routing guard perturbed the baseline → not applied; fog-visibility guard applied).
- **Verified:** GATE OK → probe-logistics 14/14, 0 pe → full no-regression GREEN (field 13/13 · bullrun 15/15 · fog 13/13 · autopause 13/13 · ai 15/15 · campaign-link 16/16 · officers 15/15 — all byte-identical; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14/14; diag-classic 346) → wcag clean (1 HUD-contrast fix). ## PHASE B-2 · OFFICERS & COMMAND on the tactical field — D65 SHIPPED + VERIFIED + PUSHED
