## TACTICAL ENGINE · P1b-iii — ROLE-AWARE AI: a smarter CONFEDERATE DEFENDER (closes "AI leans Union") SHIPPED + VERIFIED
- **What it is:** a real Confederate DEFENDER doctrine for the `__FIELD` real-time engine — the named complement to fog (D58). The shipped AI was **symmetric** (both sides ran one "advance toward the objective" heuristic), so the CS *defender* played like an attacker — the root of the logged "AI-vs-AI leans Union" gap (D57). Now `fldAiUnit` **dispatches** on `__FIELD.attacker`: the scenario DEFENDER runs the new `fldAiDefender`; the ATTACKER + BOTH sandbox sides run the verbatim-unchanged `fldAiGeneric`. In `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` + `tools/probe-ai.mjs`.
- **The doctrine (5 branches):** SURVIVAL (wavering + a stronger enemy close → fighting withdrawal to the reverse slope, still facing the threat) · COUNTERATTACK (steady + a *catchable* wavering enemy on a **dual leash** — target AND own position bounded near the objective — + local parity → charge) · DELAY (a forward delaying unit holds + fights, falls back only when locally outnumbered) · ADVANCE (a rear reinforcement marches up to the line) · HOLD (the forward face in cover, face the threat, fire). All hold points use a **stable defensive frame** (forward = crest→attacker home edge; lateral = world-x) and are **clamped inside `obj.r`** so a holding defender actually denies the hill.
- **Architecture (D60):** the SANDBOX has `attacker===null` → `fldAiDefender` is unreachable → **byte-behavior-identical** (probe-field 13/13 + golden snapshot). Unlike auto-pause, the doctrine lives in the **headless sim path**, so it is **fully probe-testable** (deterministic, no RNG). A test-only `__FIELD._aiGenericAll` (reset per launch) lets `probe-ai` A/B the doctrine vs the old AI on identical seeds.
- **Balance A/B (8 seeds, logged):** old generic AI → CS **0/8** fog-OFF, **1/8** fog-ON (the Union sweep, now empirically confirmed). Defender doctrine → CS **8/8** / **8/8**, via historical **denial/timeout** wins (the Union keeps more men but can't crack Henry House Hill in time — the 1861 shape). **Decision:** kept the corrected geometry; CS-dominant AI-vs-AI is historically faithful + the intended hard human-Union challenge; the **smarter ATTACKER AI** is the complementary next lever (not weakening the now-correct defender). A smart defender and fog are SUBSTITUTABLE (not additive) defender levers.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt:** 6 lenses × default-refute verify + a completeness critic (**27 agents, ~2.3M tokens**) → **10 confirmed (6 engine + 4 probe-fidelity), ALL FIXED**: the rotating-bearing frame collapsed the line on a flank threat + flipped the advance/hold gate (→ the **stable frame**); hold points landed outside the objective (→ **clamp inside `obj.r`**); chased uncatchable routs (→ **wavering-only**); the leash bounded only the target (→ **dual leash**); `_aiGenericAll` unreset (→ reset). Probe false-confidence: the leash/ratio sub-tests, the withdrawal-vs-delay discriminator, the bearing-flip guard, the stale header — all closed.
- **VERIFIED:** GATE OK → **probe-ai 11/11, 0 pageerrors** → full no-regression GREEN (probe-field 13/13, bullrun 15/15, fog 13/13, autopause 13/13 + strategy suite + bootprobe + t1probe + diag-classic Classic-paints, 0 pageerrors). Deliverable ≈**1509KB**.
- **NEXT:** P1b continues — the **smarter ATTACKER AI** (concentration/flanking) · the hex-mode toggle (Classic frozen) · owner-mode bridge conditioning + a tactical FREE mode · deeper 3D. Then P2–P5, loot/survival, S3–S5.

## TACTICAL ENGINE · P1b-ii — ACTIVE AUTO-PAUSE (the UG:G low-APM pillar) SHIPPED + VERIFIED
- **What it is:** the battle auto-pauses at decision points (a brigade breaks / is destroyed / reinforcements arrive) so a low-APM player keeps up — **a toggle, default ON** (the accessible default; D55). An "Auto-pause: On/Off" control-bar button + the **P** key + the persisted `G.settings.tacticalAutoPause`; the reason shows in the phase indicator + an aria-live announce + the Resume button's aria-label. In `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` + `tools/probe-autopause.mjs`.
- **Architecture (D59):** auto-pause lives **ONLY in the RAF loop** — `fldStartLoop` snapshots `{routs, alive, units}` before the fixed-timestep accumulator and calls `fldAutoPauseScan` after it. The headless probe stepper (`fldStepN`) + every `runToEnd` call `fldSimStep` directly and **never reach the scan**, so headless probes + determinism are untouched **by construction** (auto-pause sets `__FIELD.paused`, which `fldStepN` ignores). Default ON; persisted.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt:** 4 dimensions × default-refute verify + completeness critic (**10 agents**) → **4 confirmed (3 distinct), ALL FIXED**: MED turning auto-pause OFF didn't release an active pause (now releases — the escape control escapes); MED (a11y) the durable reason wasn't recoverable (now on the Resume button's aria-label); LOW same-frame death+reinforcement masked the "destroyed" reason (robust kill detection `killed = prevAlive − (aliveNow − spawned)` + combined reasons).
- **VERIFIED:** GATE OK → **probe-autopause 13/13, 0 pageerrors** (incl. the headless-unaffected + determinism invariant) → full no-regression **27 probe suites + t1probe + diag-classic (Classic paints), 0 pageerrors**; probe-field 13/13 + probe-bullrun 15/15 + probe-fog 13/13 unregressed. Deliverable ≈**1500KB**.
- **NEXT:** P1b continues — hex-mode toggle (Classic frozen) · smarter CS counterattack AI · bridge conditioning · deeper 3D. Then P2–P5, loot/survival, S3–S5.

## TACTICAL ENGINE · P1b-i — FOG OF WAR (the UG:G recon pillar) SHIPPED + VERIFIED
- **What it is:** a per-side line-of-sight visibility model on the `__FIELD` engine — **a toggle, default OFF** (D55; MODERN-UGG-PLAN §5). Fog ON: an enemy is seen only when a friendly unit is within sight range (cavalry scout widest 720yd / inf 430 / art 470) with a clear line (woods block sight); AI + targeting engage ONLY visible foes; the 2D + 3D renderers hide unscouted enemies from the US player; **last-known "ghosts"** mark where a foe was last seen (purged on death); the HUD shows only *sighted* brigades. Toggle via a "Fog" control-bar button (with `aria-pressed`) + the **V** key + the persisted `G.settings.tacticalFog`. All in `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` (shared by sandbox + Bull Run) + `tools/probe-fog.mjs`.
- **Architecture (D58):** `fldVisible(side,target)` short-circuits `true` when fog is OFF → every gate is a **no-op** and the engine is byte-behavior-identical to pre-fog (probe-field 13/13, probe-bullrun 15/15, Classic green). Fog ON: `fldComputeVisibility()` builds `__FIELD.vis` once per tick (+ primed at launch for the deploy screen); `fldLosClear` uses an **exact segment-vs-woods penetration model** (blocked past 75yd of timber — robust where a fixed-sample walk leaked at grazing chords and over-blocked two units in the same woods). Determinism: position-based, no RNG.
- **Teaching + balance:** fog ON **flips the Bull Run AI outcome to a Confederate denial win** (probe-confirmed) — the Union advances blind into the unseen reverse-slope (Jackson) + rail reserves (Early/Elzey). Historically correct AND it directly answers the D57-logged "AI-leans-Union with fog OFF" gap: fog is the defender's friend. No numbers changed (default OFF keeps prior balance).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt:** 5 dimensions × default-refute verify + completeness critic (**17 agents**) → **11 confirmed (5 root causes), ALL FIXED**: HIGH dead-enemy phantom "?" ghost (purge `lastSeen` on kill + harden the ghost guard); MED fog-ON-at-launch blacked out the DEPLOY screen (prime `vis` in `fldResetRun`); MED `fldLosClear` grazing-leak + same-woods self-block (→ exact penetration model); MED toggle missing `aria-pressed`; LOW frozen "N sighted" HUD (throttled refresh).
- **VERIFIED:** GATE OK → **probe-fog 13/13, 0 pageerrors** → full no-regression **26 probe suites + t1probe + diag-classic (Classic paints), 0 pageerrors**; probe-field 13/13 + probe-bullrun 15/15 (fog-OFF invariant holds) + a fog screenshot inspected (hidden CS reserves, sighted-count HUD, Fog:On button). Deliverable ≈**1495KB**.
- **NEXT:** P1b continues — hex-mode toggle (Classic frozen) · smarter CS counterattack AI · bridge conditioning · deeper 3D. Then P2–P5, loot/survival, S3–S5.

## TACTICAL ENGINE · P1a — the FIRST BULL RUN scenario SHIPPED + VERIFIED (the first REAL battle on the `__FIELD` engine)
- **What it is:** First Bull Run (First Manassas), July 21, 1861, brigade scale, real-time, on a **historical-terrain field** — Henry House Hill (the objective crest), Matthews Hill, Chinn Ridge, the Robinson House lane (wall cover), woods, + labeled markers (Bull Run creek, Young's Branch, the Warrenton Turnpike, Sudley Springs Ford, the Stone Bridge, "to Manassas Junction"), drawn in both 2D and 3D. **The teaching mechanic = the rail-pivot REINFORCEMENT TIMELINE:** the engaged OOB arrives in WAVES (the real engagement) — at T=0 the Union lead (Burnside, Porter) contacts the Confederate delaying force (Evans, Bee, Bartow) on Matthews Hill; both sides feed brigades over the morning; the Confederates rally on Henry Hill and receive rail-borne reinforcements — Jackson @135s ("Stonewall"), Stuart @180s, Early @220s, Elzey @275s "off the train" onto Chinn Ridge (the Union right). 9 brigades/side (2+3 at T=0, 13 in waves). Selectable from a "⚔ BATTLE — FIRST BULL RUN (1861)" menu button beside the sandbox. A pre-battle briefing modal + arrival banners + an end-screen "your war vs history" teaching payoff.
- **Architecture (D57; design judge-panel, approach A "guarded T0 seams" won 8.9 vs B 6.7 / C 7.8):** `data/bullrun.json` (engaged OOB distilled from `HISTORICAL-DATA.md`, provenance-tagged, anti-Lost-Cause) + `src/tactical/T1-bull-run.js` (orchestration only — terrain build + OOB instantiation + arrival splice; never duplicates combat math) + minimal **no-op-by-default seams** in `T0-field-sandbox.js` (keyed on `__FIELD.scenario`/`reinforce`/`attacker`, all null/"sandbox" by default → the P0 sandbox path stays byte-behavior-identical, probe-field held 13/13; a terrain golden-snapshot guards sandbox geometry). **ASYMMETRIC victory** (Union seizes the hill / CS denies to the time limit; `__FIELD.winBy` records destroy/hold/timeout). Reinforcements spawn in array order, no spawn-time RNG (determinism). A side is destroyed only with no live units AND no reinforcements still detraining.
- **Balance auto-tune (logged):** `holdToWinSec` 75→**140** + `timeLimitSec` 600→**480** — 75 let the CS auto-hold the rear objective and win at ~76s before the timeline engaged; 140 makes the full rail-pivot timeline engage (all 13 waves; battles 262–472s). The asymmetry probe proves the rail pivot is **LOAD-BEARING** (removing ONLY the CS trains drops the Confederate outcome score sharply). **KNOWN/LOGGED for P1b:** AI-vs-AI leans Union (strong attacker AI) — the primary mode is human-Union racing the timeline; CS-favorable balance (smarter defensive AI, fog-of-war toggle) is a P1b item.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (loop-until-dry):** R1 = 6 dimensions × diverse-lens default-refute verify + completeness critic (**27 agents, ~1.6M tokens**) → **14 of 20 confirmed, ALL FIXED** (HIGH: missing-`data.objective` crash; briefing-Esc-tears-down-battle; focus yanked off the briefing button; `fld3dBuildUnits` GPU-leak on each reinforcement → dispose-before-detach, probe-confirmed bounded 21 vs 51 geoms. MED/LOW: stale `scenData` title leak; rally-aware scenario gone-check; `winBy` + 4 probe gaps). R2 critic caught a REAL gameplay bug the `autoBoth`-only probe missed: **player (US) reinforcements idled in the rear** → now auto-march to the objective on arrival; + batched same-tick a11y announcements + a coordinate drift-guard. Every fix re-probed green.
- **WCAG AA (wcag-auditor on the new UI):** 8 non-text-contrast border fixes, a `:focus-visible` outline for the tactical buttons, `aria-modal` + a Tab focus-trap on the end dialog. Body text already cleared 4.5:1.
- **VERIFIED:** GATE OK → **probe-bullrun 15/15 + a 3D-geometry-leak guard, 0 pageerrors** (full engaged OOB · 3 named hills + objective + markers · reinforcements on-schedule/in-order/idempotent · player reinforcements advance · reinforcement-era reach + winBy · defender-denial timeout win · rail-pivot load-bearing asymmetry · determinism · sandbox golden-snapshot · no Classic contamination · 2D path · scenario a11y · live-menu button · 3D bounded) → **full no-regression GREEN: 25 probe suites + t1probe 14/14 + bootprobe + diag-classic Classic-paints, all 0 pageerrors**; probe-field **13/13** (P0 unregressed, post-WCAG). Deliverable ≈**1485KB**.
- **NEXT (tactical P1b):** the hex-mode toggle (Classic frozen) · smarter CS defensive/counterattack AI + the fog-of-war toggle (default OFF) · full owner-mode bridge conditioning into the scenario + a tactical-only FREE mode · deeper 3D (PBR/HDRI/post-FX). Then P2–P5, loot/survival, S3–S5.

## TACTICAL ENGINE · P0 — the real-time SANDBOX skirmish SHIPPED + VERIFIED (the D54/D55 reprioritization: tactical FIRST, ahead of S3–S5)
- **What it is:** the FIRST real-time, gridless, UG:G-style tactical layer — a **sandbox skirmish** (2 brigades a side, one procedural 3D field) that runs the full core loop end-to-end: **deploy → drag-maneuver + facing → line/column → fire → morale/rout/rally → charge → win/lose**, with low-APM controls (click-select, drag = move + face), active-pause + 1×/2×/4×, an objective-hold/army-collapse/time win, and reactive-lite enemy AI. New `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` (the new `tactical/` subsystem folder) + `tools/probe-field.mjs`. Launched from a "⚔ Tactical Sandbox (Beta)" button injected into the live broadsheet main menu (Field Dispatches column) + the global `fldLaunchSandbox()`.
- **Architecture (D56):** a **SIBLING `__FIELD` engine** with its own THREE scene + RAF loop + full-screen DOM root — NOT a mutation of the hex-bound `__M3D` 3D re-skin — so it is completely off the Classic code path (**zero regression**, probe-verified: never writes `G.battle`/`G.campaign`/`G.mode`). **Renderer-agnostic sim** (pure-data state) with a **mandatory offline 2D top-down fallback** (D54) when THREE can't load. Combat formulas **ported** from the base engine (`moraleCheck`/`resolveFire`/`resolveCharge` ~1015-1086; ratings ~10126), adapted to continuous per-tick resolution; seeded RNG for reproducible probing.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (6 dimensions × diverse-lens skeptic verify, **60 agents**, ~3.3M tokens) → **24 of 27 confirmed, all fixed** (DECISIONS **D56.0–.3** + the finding list). HIGHs: the menu button anchored on a DEAD shadowed menu (`#mmFree`/`.menu-grid`) so the whole module was UI-unreachable → re-anchored on the live broadsheet `#gnFree` + a probe MENU-ENTRY regression step; an exit-during-async-THREE-load resurrection/leak → a launch-generation token; an inoperable-by-keyboard end screen + Tab hijack → phase-guarded keys + focus move + `role=dialog`; a silently-blank 2D fallback when 3D init throws post-context → a fresh-canvas swap. MEDs incl. deploy facings pointing sideways (every front mis-scored as a flank), mutual-charge double melee, inverted column enfilade, 180°-backward 3D facing, per-frame Color alloc, color-only side ID → non-color "U"/"C" + cube/pyramid cues. LOWs incl. OrbitControls/contextLoss disposal, window-listener removal on exit, AI-clock reset, ammo taper, viewport-scale clamp, resize-flicker.
- **Balance auto-tune (logged):** `FIRE_BASE` 7.4 → **3.2** — the fight-length knob; the loop settles at ~**90s** at 1× (maneuver → firefight → morale-driven rout cascade at ~10-15% casualties, the UG:G feel, not a bloodbath).
- **VERIFIED:** `probe-field` **13/13**, 0 pageerrors, GPU-flake-free + a confirmed mid-battle 2D screenshot (with the "U"/"C" cues). Full no-regression: **24 probe suites green, 0 pageerrors, diag-classic Classic paints.** Bumped `t1probe` goto 30s→60s (the suite standard; the 1.45MB file's `load` wait exceeded the old budget — not a game regression). Deliverable ≈**1448KB**.
- **NEXT (tactical P1):** the **First Bull Run vertical slice** — scale to the real OOB (more brigades, the historical map/terrain), wire FULL strategic conditioning via the bridge + a tactical-only FREE mode, deepen the 3D (reuse PBR/HDRI/post-FX), add the hex-mode toggle (Classic stays frozen). Then fog toggle, loot/survival texture, S3–S5.

## S2 m5 · COMMAND / NAMED-GENERALS SHIPPED + VERIFIED + PUSHED — the generals you appoint, promote, and relieve now drive the army you field
- **What it is (S2 COMPLETE):** the President appoints / promotes / relieves the commanding general of his principal army. New `data/generals.json` (20 generals, US 10 / CS 10) + `src/35-command.js` + `C.president.command` + a new **"Command"** desk tab (the 13th). Each commander: traits (skill / aggression / caution), an EVOLVING reputation (win ↑ / loss ↓), and ambition (the McClellan problem). A date-aware DEFAULT holds the post (the iconic-army chain — US Scott→McClellan→Burnside→Hooker→Meade→Grant; CS J.E. Johnston→Lee); appointing locks it; relieving a popular general costs political capital, with a free "restore the historical command" escape.
- **THE KEY WIRING (the milestone's point):** `commandLeadership(C)` (= `0.55·skill + 0.45·reputation` blended with `cabinetLeadership`, **anchored at 64**) finally drives the bridge LEADERSHIP facet — the `var leadership = 64;` placeholder live since the battle layer (D49.7). `bridgeArmy.overall` gains a bidirectional leadership edge (±, 0 at the anchor → fresh/default command = byte-equivalent Classic); the general's temperament also nudges the auto-resolve margin (`commandMarginEdge`). The m3 leader-morale layer deliberately STAYS on `cabinetLeadership` (D53 decoupling — no double-count, no confound of the cabinet-isolating morale probe).
- **Content:** the web-grounded `s2-generals-research` workflow (10 agents: 4 research + 4 adversarial-verify + balance + teaching cards) → 20 generals + 4 multi-voice teaching cards. **Anti-Lost-Cause:** Lee excellent-not-infallible; Grant/Sherman/Thomas top-tier; **Forrest's bio NAMES Fort Pillow + the KKK + slave-trading**; Bragg/Hood poor army commanders.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (8 dimensions × skeptic verify, **20 agents**) → **9 of 12 confirmed, all fixed** (DECISIONS **D53.1–.10**). The HIGHs: a `bridgeArmy↔cabinet` recursion landmine (→ a `_brgLeadGuard` re-entrancy guard), Thomas (Western) wrongly defaulting the US chain (→ nulled, like Sherman), and the post-war fallback jumping to the first commander (→ latest-end continuity). MED: `_activeId` save-validation, capital-rounding soft-lock, `_cmdTraitBar`/wire-id escaping.
- **VERIFIED:** probe-command **14/14** (incl. the fresh-anchor Classic-safety + the recursion-guard & post-war regression guards); full no-regression GREEN — bridge 6/6 · conditioning 6/6 · auto-resolve 7/7 · cabinet 12/12 · morale 10/10 · desk 13/13 · all 16+ suites + diag-classic; **0 pageerrors** throughout. Deliverable ≈1392KB.
- **Standing instruction (Aaron, this session):** push to **github.com/adhanke-star/History-Video-Game** per milestone ONLY after PROPER VETTING (GATE OK + full no-regression + diag-classic + 0 pageerrors + bug-hunt-fixed). Codified across MEMORY + START-HERE + AUTONOMOUS-RUN (DECISIONS **D53-OPS**); the stale "no remote / local-only" lines retired.

## S2 m4 · THE PRESS / PUBLIC-OPINION SYSTEM SHIPPED + VERIFIED — the real newspapers react to your war and drive the public will
- **What it is:** 12 real Civil War papers, North and South, react to your war's turns with period broadsheet editorials. New `data/press.json` + `src/34-press.js` + `C.press` + a new **"The Press"** desk tab (the 12th). Each paper has a real political LEAN (radical / administration / war-democrat / copperhead / fire-eater / abolitionist) that sets how it reacts; `pressOnResolve` (before `moraleOnResolve`) reads the turn's condition (victory / defeat / stalemate / heavy-casualties / emancipation-once), each paper runs a matching editorial and shifts its FAVOR (±8 clamped, or drifts toward its lean), and the aggregate SENTIMENT feeds `moraleCompute`'s public-will layer (anchored at 50). So the press is a real driver of the home front that decides the 1864 election.
- **Content:** the web-grounded `s2-press-research` workflow (7 agents, WebSearch/WebFetch + adversarial verify) → 12 real papers with real editors + URLs: Greeley's *Tribune*, Garrison's *Liberator*, Medill's *Chicago Tribune*, Curtis's *Harper's Weekly*; the *NY World*/*Chicago Times*/*Crisis*/*Herald* Copperhead-Democratic sheets; the *Richmond Examiner* & *Charleston Mercury* savaging Davis, the *Enquirer* defending him, the *Dispatch*. Anti-Lost-Cause throughline: BOTH presses were bitterly divided; the Confederate press was no monolith.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses × 3-skeptic verify, **44 agents**) → **7 of 13 confirmed**, all fixed (DECISIONS **D52.1–.7**). The MED: a corrupt-save `null` headline entry crashed the Press tab (→ `pressInit` filters headline entries). Plus NaN-sentiment guards, the emancipation-fired latch, the heavy-casualties dampener, winner-consistency.
- **VERIFIED:** probe-press **10/10**; probe-desk **13/13** (the new Press tab); probe-morale **10/10** (the `pressTerm` coupling anchored = no change); full no-regression green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable ≈1300KB.
- **Tooling lesson:** never run two browser-probe batteries concurrently — they collide on the shared `:8765` server + `tools/shots/*.json` (ERR_CONNECTION_REFUSED / goto-timeout flakes). Run batteries SEQUENTIALLY.
- **NEXT: S2 m5** — command: appoint/promote/relieve generals + the named-generals system (§8.24/§8.58/D31.4/D38.2); wire `cabinetLeadership` + generals → the bridge leadership facet (the `src/85` ~line 90 `leadership=64` placeholder).

## S2 m3 · THE THREE-LAYER MORALE SYSTEM + the 1864 election hinge SHIPPED + VERIFIED — troop / leader / public will, and the home front that decides the war
- **What it is:** three interacting, visible morale layers, surfaced as **"The Nation's Will"** in the War Effort overview. New `src/33-morale.js` + `C.morale`. `moraleCompute` derives each layer fresh each turn with the interactions baked in: **troop** (battle conditioning + supply, lifted by leadership), **leader** (win-rate + the sitting cabinet's `cabinetLeadership`, dragged by an active ambition tell), **public will** (sunk by the accumulating casualty toll [D35.6 human cost] + runaway inflation, lifted by victories + the South's hope of recognition). Plus an **1864-election forecast** mirroring the frozen clock's support formula.
- **The 1864 election → the war's end (D41.2):** the frozen clock already resolves the referendum from weariness/capital/win-rate; m3 adds the consequence — when the verdict lands (once), it feeds the existing `enemyWill` system: **re-elected → enemyWill −8** (you grind the enemy toward your negotiated-peace win), **repudiated → enemyWill +12 + a durable public-will hit** (the home front broke; the enemy takes heart). You can win every battle and still lose the war if the public will fails.
- **Design discipline:** morale is a computed READOUT with exactly ONE bounded sim coupling (the one-time election→enemyWill nudge) — it writes nothing to the frozen clock/economy/manpower, so it can't regress their assertions; the coupling feeds the EXISTING victory module (enemyWill→victoryReady).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses × 3-skeptic verify, **29 agents**) → **7 of 8 confirmed** (1 refuted, validating the no-regression), all fixed (DECISIONS **D51.1–.6**). The HIGHs: the election latch wasn't migration-safe (a legacy save past 1864 would re-fire the nudge → seed it from `resolved1864`) and was burned before the effect landed (→ atomic with application).
- **VERIFIED:** probe-morale **10/10** (layers + interactions + the election consequence both directions + corrupt/legacy-save hardening); full no-regression green — **probe-victory 12/12** (the enemyWill coupling REINFORCES its assertions), all 16 other suites + diag-classic Classic paints; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable ≈1249KB.
- **NEXT: S2 m4** — the press / public-opinion system (§8.57/D38.1): period papers react → public morale + the 1864 election; censorship/Vallandigham as a lever; ties the broadsheet UI to the 3-layer morale.

## S2 m2 · CURATED EXECUTIVE DECISIONS + the pendingChoices loop SHIPPED + VERIFIED — emancipation as a dated decision, civil-liberties dilemmas, a non-blocking decision deck
- **What it is:** the S0 `pendingChoices` stub becomes a real decision system. New `data/decisions.json` (8 cards) + `src/32-decisions.js`. Cards surface in the between-battles interstitial AND a new **"Decisions" desk tab** (the 11th); the engine (`decOnResolve`) owns the queue at the §8.68 cadence (≤2 new non-hinge/turn; the hinge always surfaces) and `decResolve` applies bounded, clamped, logged effects. The marquee is **EMANCIPATION** — a dated Union hinge (issue / go-radical-now / refuse) that sets `C.president.emancipation`, which the **manpower module reads to gate the USCT pool** (issue → unlocks, even pre-1863 if radical; refuse → never; no decision → the historical 1863 default, zero regression). Plus civil-liberties + home-front cards both sides: habeas corpus (US + CS), Vallandigham, the NYC draft riots, press censorship, the Richmond bread riot, the twenty-slave law.
- **Content:** the web-grounded `s2-decisions-research` workflow (17 agents, WebSearch/WebFetch + adversarial verify) → real public sources with URLs (National Archives, Library of Congress, the Freedmen & Southern Society Project, Dickinson's House Divided; Neely, McCurry, Foner, Oakes; the Greeley/Browning/Corning letters). Anti-Lost-Cause, Black-agency-centered (Du Bois's general strike; the twenty-slave law's "rich man's war"). Merged conservatively (scaffold cards' ids/effects preserved) + entity-normalized.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses × 3-skeptic verify, **56 agents**) → **12 of 17 confirmed**, all fixed (DECISIONS **D50.1–.12**). The HIGHs: `decResolve` lacked an idempotency guard (a card could be re-resolved, flipping emancipation AFTER the USCT pool was irreversibly banked) → resolved cards are now terminal + pending-gated; and the applier upper-clamped capital at 100 while the frozen clock treats it as unbounded-above (the 1864 referendum reads it) → capital is now floor-only. Plus cross-module save-integrity (manpower sanitizes emancipation before reading it), queue dedup + eligibility re-validation, and id-sanitization.
- **VERIFIED:** probe-decisions **14/14** (schema + dup-id gate, side/year eligibility, cadence cap, persistence, resolve+effects+dequeue, the emancipation→USCT gate in all 3 cases, idempotency, capital floor-only, corrupt-save hardening, render+wire); probe-desk **13/13** (the new Decisions tab); probe-manpower **9/9** (USCT-gate no-regression); diag-classic Classic paints; full no-regression green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable ≈1237KB.
- **NEXT: S2 m3** — 3-layer morale (troop / leader-reputation / public-will-decides-late §8.67) wired to the 1864 election hinge (§8.61/D39.2).

## S2 m1 · THE CABINET & ADVISOR SYSTEM SHIPPED + VERIFIED — the full historical cabinet, date-aware churn, and the one-line-rec / Heed-or-Delegate / why / ambition advisor UX (R25 linchpin)
- **What it is:** the S0 4-secretary stub becomes the FULL historical cabinet per side. New `data/cabinet.json` (US 13 / CS 15 advisors) + `src/31-cabinet.js` (overrides `presRenderCabinet`/`presWireCabinet`; `cabInit`/`cabOnResolve` registered in `90-president-register.js`). The roster is **date-aware**: the current holder of each office is whoever historically held it at the strategic date, so the CHURN plays out mechanically as the war advances — Davis's revolving War office (Walker→Benjamin→Randolph→Seddon→Breckinridge), Benjamin's three-post rotation (War→State), Chase out July 1864, Cameron→Stanton. Each of the 4 principal advisors gives a one-line **recommendation keyed to the war state**, a one-click **Heed** (a bounded, logged, once-per-turn nudge) or **Delegate**, an expandable **why** (reasoning + teaching + provenance), and an **ambition tell** that surfaces for the self-servers (Chase, Toombs, Blair) but not the loyal (Welles, Mallory). A full-roster expander makes the churn legible; two cross-cutting cards teach the team-of-rivals vs Confederate-governance-dysfunction contrast.
- **Content:** the `s2-cabinet-research` workflow — **21 agents, web-grounded, two adversarial-verify passes** (1.1M tokens) → 18 principal profiles + cross-cards, citing real scholarship (Stahr's *Seward*/*Stanton*, Howard Jones, Ferris, Owsley, Ball's *Financial Failure*, Levine's *Confederate Emancipation*, Rable, Goodwin) + primary sources (Seward's April 1 memo). Merged conservatively into `cabinet.json` (structure/tenures/condition-vocabulary preserved; verified voice/ambition/stance-prose/cards grafted), then entity-normalized so the render layer escapes exactly once. Unflinching + anti-Lost-Cause: Benjamin's antisemitic scapegoating, Memminger's structural finance collapse, Davis's micromanagement and the states'-rights paralysis (Brown & Vance) as real causes of defeat.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses × 3-skeptic independent verify, **62 agents**, 4.1M tokens) → **8 confirmed of 19 (11 refuted)**, all fixed (DECISIONS **D49.1–.8**): the two HIGHs were (1) a corrupt/imported save with a primitive `president`/`date` crashing the cabinet tab under `"use strict"` — hardened `presInit` + a render try/catch; and (2) cross-domain **Heed-stacking flooding political capital** (which feeds the 1864 reelection referendum) — gated the capital gain to **once per turn total**. Plus an array-`cabinetState` dead-UI guard, a tenure-predecessor fix for multi-tenure date-leaps, a CS-AG tenure-gap data fix, a navy micro-effect, a log-escaping hardening, and a scope-confirm that `cabinetLeadership` is **not yet consumed by the bridge** (so zero battle-balance change this milestone — leadership wiring deferred to the generals milestone where it's the headline).
- **VERIFIED:** probe-cabinet **12/12** (data load, date-aware churn both sides, condition-keyed stance selection, ambition activation, the once-per-turn Heed cap, corrupt-save hardening, the multi-tenure predecessor, render + wire); **full no-regression green** — diag-classic Classic paints (nonBlank 346); desk 12/12 (updated to the new advisor UX); conditioning 6/6, auto-resolve 7/7, bridge 6/6, economy 8/8, victory 12/12, blockade 11/11, manpower 9/9, production 4/4, cannon 9/9, engineering 9/9, cover 8/8, armory-field 9/9, targeting 5/5; 0 pageerrors throughout. Deliverable ≈1130KB.
- **NEXT: S2 m2** — curated decision cards + the `president.pendingChoices` loop (emancipation as a dated Union decision §8.27 + civil-liberties dilemmas §8.62), `data/decisions.json`, web-grounded research.

# RUN-LOG — 2026-06-14 (run j, Opus 4.8 — the BATTLE LAYER: A1 Cannon Corps → A2…→ S2–S5 → tactical)

**Context:** Overnight autonomous run under the §8 charter (D30–D41). Battle layer first (A1→A6), then the strategic arc S2→S5, then tactical P0–P5. GitHub backup authorized (`adhanke-star/History-Video-Game`, private). Ultracode on; adversarial bug-hunt before every commit; decide-&-log every fork.

## A1 · THE CANNON CORPS SHIPPED + VERIFIED — buildable field artillery + the CS asymmetry made mechanical
- **What it is:** "The Cannon Corps" block appended below The Armory tab. You raise real Civil War field batteries with `C.funds` (12-pdr Napoleon, 3-inch Ordnance Rifle, 10-pdr Parrott, Whitworth [rare import], 12-pdr howitzer — `data/artillery.json`, from an 11-agent verified research workflow), loot-tiered common→rare. A battery is a big-ticket buy (Napoleon ~$900) raised by the BATTERY (the corps you assemble), unlike the Armory's small-arms-by-fraction. The corps' battery-score (gun quality × park coverage, with the CS handicaps) feeds the battle bridge as a new **artillery** facet that adds punch to the army you field.
- **Found + scaffolded by the prior session** (`src/56-artillery.js`, wiring into manifest / `_t1InitAll` / the Armory tab / the bridge `bridgeArmy`, `tools/probe-cannon.mjs`); this session BUILT → PROBED → bug-hunted → hardened → committed it as the first run-j milestone.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (workflow: 5 lenses × independent verify, 21 agents) → 9 confirmed real findings, all fixed (DECISIONS D42): array-guard save-corruption holes in `artInit` (the big one — a JSON round-trip would silently wipe the park), battery-count sanitization, the **cosmetic 4-vs-6 handicap made mechanical** (CS batteries now fill the park ~2/3 as fast + CS-only fuze/horse/mixed-caliber maluses + the 1863 massing bonus with a Union Reserve edge), the Whitworth no longer cheapest-for-the-Union, and the usual hardening (cost-0 honored, no-id guard, data escaping, `n` coercion).
- **VERIFIED:** probe-cannon **9/9** + a new US>CS divergence assertion (1863, 6× howitzer12: **US 44 vs CS 33**, CS not crushed to baseline — accessible default). Bridge artillery facet 8→63, overall 76→83. No-regression: diag-classic Classic paints, probe-desk 12/12, probe-weapons 8/8, probe-bridge 6/6; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable 905.6KB.

## A2 · THE ENGINEERING WORKS CORPS SHIPPED + VERIFIED — Haupt's USMRR as a buildable arm + the rail-repair-that-can't-rebuild
- **What it is:** the third buildable in The Armory (below the Cannon Corps). Raise four engineer capabilities in levels 0-3 with funds — **Construction Corps** (Haupt's USMRR rail/bridge repair), **Field Fortifications** (the spade), **Pontoon Train** (river crossings), **Siege Works** (saps/parallels). New `src/57-engineering.js` + `data/engineering.json` + `C.engineering`. Feeds the battle bridge as an additive **engineering** facet; construction also raises the bridge supply facet, pontoons lower fatigue, and the Construction Corps repairs rail each turn — but only a *fraction* of the loss, so it SLOWS (never stops) the South's irreversible rail collapse. CS pays a 1.25× materials premium (Union engineering vastly outstripped the South's).
- **Content:** 8-agent research+verify workflow → 4 Verified multi-voice teaching cards (USMRR / fieldworks / pontoons / siege), anti-Lost-Cause and myth-correcting (Solonick "dug out not starved out"; Griffith-vs-Hess on the rifle musket; Rhea on the Cold Harbor "7,000 in minutes" myth). Citations independently fact-checked.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses × verify, 19 agents) → 5 confirmed findings, all fixed (DECISIONS D43). The important one: the rail-repair math reached a **stable equilibrium and pinned rail at 100** once the rail War-Room node was funded — contradicting the locked "irreversible decay" intent. Fixed by clawing back only a sub-1.0 fraction of the actual per-turn loss (prod stashes `railLossLast`). Plus NaN/negative guards, boolean-coercion + attribute-escaping hardening (parity fixes back-ported to A1's artillery).
- **VERIFIED:** probe-engineering **9/9** (incl. an equilibrium-regression assertion: with construction + rail node maxed, rail 100→84 declining, vs 55 without). Engineering facet 12→96; overall +10. Full no-regression green (diag-classic Classic paints, production/cannon/bridge/desk/weapons all pass); 0 pageerrors. Deliverable ≈947KB.

## A3 · TERRAIN COVER HIERARCHY SHIPPED + VERIFIED — the first frozen-engine override, the historical battlefields fight like what they were
- **What it is:** six named cover types — Stone Wall, Entrenchments, Sunken Road, Boulders, Dense Forest, Rail Fence — slotted into the frozen battle engine's EXISTING terrain/defense model. New `src/58-terrain-cover.js` + `data/terrain-cover.json`.
- **How (no fire-function override — lowest risk):** combat already divides fire damage by `TERRAIN[tile.t].def`; the `.cover` field was dead. The module MUTATES the frozen consts `TERRAIN`/`TCOL`/`PALETTE` to install the six cover types (real def values + period colors), so combat picks them up automatically (a stone wall halves casualties). It OVERRIDES `authoredMap` (verbatim base body + a decoration pass) to stamp cover onto the historical features the maps already label (Sunken Road, Marye's Heights, Devil's Den, the Round Tops, the woods, the redans). 11 stamps across 6 of 10 authored maps; positions already `fort` (Vicksburg redans, the Bloody Lane) are correctly left.
- **First frozen-engine override (§8.2):** gated hard by diag-classic — Classic paints unchanged (nonBlank 346). Revert-on-regression posture honored.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses × verify, 13 agents) → 2 medium findings fixed (DECISIONS D44): the matcher's bare `"trench"` accidentally hit "The Retrenchment" (anchored to `"trenches"`/`"retrenchment"`), and the terrain swap silently changed movement cost incl. one high-ground speedup (fixed with stonewall cost→2 + a no-speedup guard; docs reframed as an honest terrain swap). Const-mutation timing/idempotency probed and confirmed safe.
- **VERIFIED:** probe-cover **8/8** (def ladder, render colors, label matching, never-weaken, the terrain-swap invariant [11 stamps: 0 weaker, 0 faster], combat reduction); diag-classic Classic paints; full no-regression green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable ≈962KB.

## A4 · ARMORY → BATTLEFIELD SHIPPED + VERIFIED — the weapons you buy are what your brigades fire
- **What it is:** the small arms bought in The Armory (`C.armory.loadout`) become what the player's brigades carry and fire on the day. New `src/59-armory-field.js` (frozen-engine override of `genForce`).
- **How:** a unit's firepower = `WEAPONS[u.weapon].pow`. The override re-arms a fraction of the player's fresh infantry from the loadout, mapped armory-id → engine WEAPONS key (quality-monotonic). Buy Spencers → a slice of the line carries "spencer" (pow 2.05 vs the musket 1.00 = +105% fire); the rest keep standard issue, veterans keep their earned weapon, the enemy is untouched.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses × verify, 16 agents) → 5 findings fixed (DECISIONS D45). The big one (HIGH, a Classic regression): the re-arm fired whenever a campaign was merely in memory, so a **Free Battle could arm the AI enemy with the player's arsenal** — fixed by gating on `campaignCore` (the engine's own player-in-campaign discriminator). Plus an engine-era gate (no fielding arms before the engine's era) and a float-drift snap.
- **VERIFIED:** probe-armory-field **9/9** (monotonic mapping, player-not-enemy, fraction, whole-army float-safe, veterans keep weapon, Spencer +105% pow, off-campaign no-op, era-gate, Free-Battle isolation); diag-classic Classic paints (no regression from the `genForce` override); full no-regression green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable ≈970KB.

## A5 · TARGETING VERIFIED — the player already picks specific fire targets (no engine change)
- **Finding:** the frozen engine ALREADY supports full player target choice. `fireTargets(u)` returns the in-range visible enemies; `onHexClick` fires at the exact clicked hex (`resolveFire(sel,c,r)`) in fire mode — the player chooses, not an auto-pick (only the AI uses `chooseBestFireTarget`); targets are highlighted (2D + 3D); keyboard aiming works (F→arrows→Enter).
- **VERIFIED (probe-targeting 5/5):** two enemies in range → both targetable; fire mode highlights them; clicking ONE damages THAT enemy (512→483) and not the other; firing unit marked fired; already-fired unit has no targets. Doubles as a post-A1–A4 battle smoke test.
- **Decision:** ship NO engine change — the feature is complete; adding redundant UI to a working engine is over-engineering (§27) + needless override risk. A5 satisfied by verification. Optional highlight/tooltip polish deferred.

## A6a · BATTLE-DAY CONDITIONING SHIPPED + VERIFIED — the strategic war shapes the army that takes the field
- **What it is:** `src/86-battle-conditioning.js` overrides `startBattleRuntime` (frozen-engine §8.2) to apply the bridge's conditioned army to the LIVE battle (campaign battles only). The player force is scaled by `bridgeArmy(C)` (strength ×[0.88..1.12], morale shift), `C.battlePrep` is applied (entrench/forced-march/raid-supply), and Field Fortifications (A2) stamp trench cover (A3) on the line when you entrench — closing A2→A3→the battlefield end-to-end.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses × verify, 15 agents) → 4 findings fixed (DECISIONS D47). The key one (§27): a fresh campaign's `bridgeArmy.overall` is ~74-76 not 50, so the original anchor silently buffed every no-investment army +10% — re-anchored so a fresh army plays ≈ Classic (ratio 1.009). Plus a narrowed band, the auto-trench gated on the entrench order (no free over-stack), a procedural-map fallback, and objective-tile preservation.
- **VERIFIED:** probe-conditioning **6/6** (strong-war 6547 vs weak 5562; free-battle untouched; entrench +2 ent; raid-supply enemy morale 79→73; fresh≈Classic ratio 1.009; fortifications trench 68/91 when entrenching, 0 without); diag-classic Classic paints (no regression from the `startBattleRuntime` override); full no-regression green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable ≈977KB.
- **NEXT: A6b** — the bridge AUTO-RESOLVE (resolve a battle from `bridgeArmy` + variance → casualties/clock/enemyWill via `campaignAdvance`), so the owner-mode war is playable end-to-end without fighting every tactical battle.

## A6b · BRIDGE AUTO-RESOLVE SHIPPED + VERIFIED — ⚑ THE BATTLE LAYER (A1–A6) IS COMPLETE; the owner-mode war is PLAYABLE END-TO-END
- **What it is:** `src/87-auto-resolve.js` + an "Auto-resolve" button in the pre-battle briefing. Resolve a battle from the army your whole war fielded — without playing the tactical fight; "To the Field" remains. It builds the A6a-conditioned battle, decides the outcome (your edge over baseline vs the enemy + variance), then drives the engine's OWN `campaignAdvance` so the war feeds back (manpower/clock/strategy/enemyWill/victory/funds/roster) IDENTICALLY to a fought battle.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses × verify, 24 agents) → 11 findings, 6 fixes (DECISIONS D48). The big one: the original margin made a competent Union NEVER lose (auto-resolve easier than fighting, a foregone conclusion) — re-anchored on the edge-over-baseline so a baseline army is a real gamble and auto-resolve is outcome-equivalent to fighting. Plus the battle-audio teardown (was playing over the result screen), flipAtk recovery, XP parity, casualty/funds parity.
- **VERIFIED:** probe-auto-resolve **7/7** (strong war wins at margin 11, weak loses at −28 = real jeopardy; loser bleeds more; kills credited; flipAtk honored; campaignAdvance advances idx + feeds the tick); diag-classic Classic paints; full no-regression green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable ≈987KB.
- **The loop is closed:** pick a side → run economy/production/blockade/diplomacy/manpower/the three buildable corps on the President's Desk → field a conditioned army → auto-resolve or fight each battle (weapons + terrain cover + conditioning all real) → results drive the war → win via the chain or a path-to-victory + the "your war vs history" framing. **NEXT: the strategic arc S2–S5.**

## S1c SHIPPED + VERIFIED — cotton, the blockade & foreign recognition
- `src/60-blockade.js` (`G.campaign.blockade`) models the three Confederate traps as an EMERGENT arc: **(1) the 1861 King-Cotton self-embargo** (on by default for CS) earns ~0 revenue against a glutted Britain — a trap that drains the treasury; auto-expires by 1862. **(2) the blockade stranglehold** — capture-prob schedule 0.10→0.33, runner success 0.90→0.67, ports fall (Wilmington/Fort Fisher Jan 1865 → ocean sealed) → a **dynamic `importFactor`** that gates CS small-arms, **wiring the S1b `prodOnResolve` placeholder** (off > full late-war, probe-confirmed). **(3) foreign recognition** rises with the Lancashire famine + early CS wins, capped by substitution, **foreclosed after Antietam/Emancipation (1863+)** → pulls `clock.intervention` toward the low recognition reality (King Cotton can't buy intervention no battlefield bluff refills). Cotton revenue → `C.funds`. **Blockade-depth toggle** (full/flat/off, R14). ## S1d SHIPPED + VERIFIED — manpower, conscription & the replacement-ratio collapse (the war-ender)
- `src/70-manpower.js` (`G.campaign.manpower`) models the decisive demographic asymmetry: the Union refills its armies (deep 4M pool + ~25% immigrant inflow + a one-time **+180k USCT pool at Emancipation 1863** from the South's own labor base) and **replaces every casualty**; the Confederacy's **replacement ratio collapses 0.9→0.6→0.3→0.1** by 1865 (no immigration; won't arm the 3.5M enslaved) → its armies melt. Union draft = a **coercive STIMULUS** to volunteering (×1.2; only ~6% direct, Geary), CS conscription load-bearing (1862, a year earlier), age-band widening 18-35→17-50 as a crisis 'tell'; CS desertion rises with home-front distress. `C.manpower.strength` (0-100) is **the army-strength index the S5 pre-battle bridge will read.** Surfaced as a "The Ranks" block in the War Effort overview (delegated to the Sec. of War; ambient teaching). Registered after prod (reads `B.casualties` + year); no new overrides.
- **Content-complete:** 11-agent research+verify+audit workflow → `data/manpower-teaching.json` (5 multi-voice cards — Geary/Murdock/Moore/Anbinder/Lonn/Glatthaar/Levine; Black Americans as full agents, Lost Cause erasure countered; the draft-as-stimulus, the Twenty-Slave Law, commutation-as-price-ceiling, the impossibility of CS Black enlistment) + a 9-claim audit (7 CONFIRMED, 1 DISPUTED [the 0.9→0.1 ratios are direction-confirmed but not a published statistic — kept as calibrated `_inferred` values], 1 CORRECTED [date precision only]). **No sim data correction needed** (unlike S1c's Erlanger fix). Digest folded into the card store + `HISTORICAL-DATA-DIPLOMACY.md` lineage.
- **VERIFIED (probe-manpower 9/9 — FULL `_t1Resolve`, 20 turns to 1865):** US strength **holds 100** / pool 4000→2082 (deep) / USCT unlocks 1863 / ~2,098k enlisted (≈ real 2.13M ceiling) vs CS ratio **0.9→0.1** / strength 99→**53 (melting)** / pool→**0** / desertion→**145k** / ~933k enlisted. The dying-Confederacy overview (1865) reads Ragged equipment 14 · Army strength 15 · weariness 100 · foreign-intervention 0 — every system interlocking. Regression: probe-desk 12/12, probe-economy 8/8, probe-production 4/4, probe-blockade 11/11, diag-classic Classic paints; 0 pageerrors. New gate `tools/probe-manpower.mjs`.

**S1 COMPLETE (a/b/c/d).** The full asymmetric economy is built: finance/inflation · production/logistics · cotton/blockade/diplomacy · manpower/conscription — all emergent, content-complete, probe-verified, interlinked through `clock.weariness`/`clock.intervention`/`C.funds` and now producing an army-strength index for the battle bridge.

# RUN-LOG — 2026-06-13 (run g, Opus 4.8 — CINEMATIC GRAPHICS RUN, fresh VS Code session)

**Context:** Executing `GRAPHICS-RUN-PROMPT.md` §D — take the Modern 3D renderer to a high-end, stylized-realistic, cinematic finished look. Single-file / $0 / free-CC0 / full-autonomy / Ultracode on. Phase 0 verified: Blender 4.5.10 bridge LIVE (keys re-applied from `secrets.local.json` — PolyHaven/Sketchfab/Hyper3D FAL_AI), real-GPU verify confirmed (`shot-gpu.mjs` GL renderer = `ANGLE Metal Renderer: Intel(R) UHD 617`, NOT SwiftShader), splice anchor `/*__ENGINE_END__*/` unique, node 25.9. Research fan-out (4 agents + adversarial verify) banked the r0.128 post-FX load order, Poly Haven shortlist, period unit dossier, wet-plate grade GLSL.

## G1 — CINEMATIC POST-PROCESSING ✅ SHIPPED + GPU-verified
`chunks/out/M3D_POSTFX.js` — lazy EffectComposer stack on the SAME jsdelivr three@0.128 tree (15 example scripts, dependency-correct load order **adversarially verified**: caught two real load-time deps — r128 `SMAAPass` needs `SMAAShader.js`, `BokehPass` needs `BokehShader.js` — that a naive list omits → black screen). **ACES tone-map** (renderer.toneMapping=4) + **UnrealBloom** (high threshold 0.88 so daylit grass/sky don't fog) + **period wet-plate grade** ShaderPass (cool steel shadows / warm-khaki mids / ivory highlights, sat pull, S-curve) + **SMAA** + **film-grain+vignette** ShaderPass. **PERF-TIERED for UHD 617:** LOW = direct ACES render (no composer); AUTO (desktop default) = bloom+grade+SMAA+vignette (sprite-safe); HIGH = +SSAO (kernelRadius 16) +grain; DOF/Bokeh implemented but opt-in (`__M3D.postDOF`, default off — blurs the tactical read). reduceMotion freezes/zeroes grain. **Trap avoided:** grade/grain shader defs use `new THREE.Color/Vector2`, so they're built by FACTORY FNS at composer time, never at chunk eval (THREE loads async AFTER the spliced script — a top-level `new THREE.*` would throw and kill the whole game). Override-by-redeclaration of `_m3dStartLoop`+`_m3dResize` (last wins; both replicate prior body + add composer); a guarded `_m3dFrameUpdate(dt,now)` hook lets G4/G5 plug the loop without re-overriding. New tool `tools/shot-postfx.mjs` waits for the composer to actually build (post scripts async) then shoots the true full-stack frame + reports pass list. **Verified:** auto passes=[Render,Bloom,grade,SMAA,grain], high=[Render,SSAO,Bloom,grade,SMAA,grain], toneMapping=4, 0 pageerrors, no washout (r128 encoding gotcha did NOT bite), no SSAO sprite-halos at gameplay zoom.

## G2 — HDRI SKIES ✅ SHIPPED + GPU-verified
3 Poly Haven CC0 HDRIs (2k, verified `#?RADIANCE`) → `assets/3d/env/`: `sky_day.hdr` (syferfontein_18d_clear_puresky), `sky_overcast.hdr` (overcast_soil_puresky), `sky_dusk.hdr` (belfast_sunset_puresky), via direct PolyHaven CDN fetch (file-naming needs exact names; Blender import drops into the scene, not my asset dir — direct fetch is the right tool, still CC0/$0). `chunks/out/M3D_HDRI_SELECT.js` re-declares `_m3dLoadEnv` + `_m3dApplyAtmosphere` (winning; atmosphere body replicated verbatim + one `_m3dSelectEnv()` call) → the sky now picks rain/fog/snow→overcast, dawn/dusk→dusk, else day, cached PMREM per name. **GPU-verified:** clear→bright daylit sky; rain→cohesive grey overcast sky + grey light (was an odd near-black before — the day HDRI under storm fog/grade).

(A) **Weather** — rain streaks / drifting snow as a camera-following recycled Points volume driven by `G.battle.wx`, perf-tiered counts (high 1700/1100, auto 850/600, low 0), reduceMotion-off. Muzzle/cannon flash already blooms (fire FX is additive bright, above the 0.88 bloom threshold). **GPU-verified:** rain falls under the overcast sky (0 err); seeded 16 fire events → 18 live banks visible as drifting powder smoke over the line (`shot-postfx.mjs` gained `wx` + `fx` args). reduceMotion + low tier verified off.

(My 6 chunks are `_m3d*` + additive CSS; the classic 2D `draw()` path is structurally untouched.) This harness bug predated my session and would have masked real Classic regressions in any run since run-f.

## TRACK C — Adaptive period audio score ✅ SHIPPED + verified
`chunks/out/AUDIO_SCORE.js` (Opus executor, ~810 lines) + `chunks/out/AUDIO_WIRE.js` (my glue). Own AudioContext (never touches the existing SOUND IIFE), lookahead scheduler. API: `scoreInit / musicStart(menu|march|battle|camp) / musicStop / bugleCall(reveille|assembly|charge|recall|taps|to_the_colors|tattoo) / dinSet / dinStop / scoreSampleBattle`. **Content:** original C-major fife-and-drum quickstep (menu/march), low detuned-saw drone + slow drum + sparse bugle (battle, mixed under the din), lonely triangle air (camp); **bugle calls = harmonic-series pitches ONLY** (valveless-bugle fact); **battle din** = brown-noise rumble + cannon thumps + musket crackle whose density/gain scale with combat intensity. Gated on `G.settings.sound` + new `G.settings.music` (default on; Settings toggle added). **Hooks (guarded core edits I own):** `_audEnterBattle` at `startBattleRuntime` tail (music+din+ambient + a 1.2s `dinSet(scoreSampleBattle())` sampler), `_audLeaveBattle`+win/loss bugle (`to_the_colors`/`taps`) in `endBattle`, charge bugle in `resolveCharge` (player only), `_audMenu` in the newspaper `openMainMenu`. **Also fixed a latent gap:** `ambientStart()` was only ever called from the Settings toggle — now starts on battle entry.
- **Audit caught 2 real executor bugs + I caught a 3rd that nearly shipped:** (1+2) `scoreSampleBattle` guessed `G.battle` field names — fixed to the real shape (`casualties:{US,CS}` uppercase; engagement via `u.fired`). (3) **CRITICAL — the whole module gated on `window.G`, but `G` is `const G` (lexical global, NOT a `window` property) → `window.G` is `undefined` → `sndOn()` always false → the entire score was silently muted.** Fixed: `window.G`→bare `G` (the IIFE closes over the outer const). The empirical `tools/audioprobe.mjs` caught it — a static read had passed it twice.
- **LESSON (banked, recurring):** this game declares `G` (and `HEX`, etc.) with `const`/`let` at script top-level → they are **lexical globals, NOT on `window`**. Reference them by **bare name**, never `window.G`. Same trap bit `tools/bootprobe.mjs`. Any appended chunk that reads engine state must use bare `G`.
- **Gates:** full parse PASS; hex 0; no dup symbols; `tools/audioprobe.mjs` (real Chrome WebAudio) — API present, `scoreSampleBattle` 0→0.64 on a real casualty bump, battle entry+exit with the full score live = ZERO pageerrors; `tools/bootprobe.mjs` — default boots **Modern 3D + audio together**, 32 units, zero real errors. (I cannot hear it — musicality is Aaron's ear-test, the audio analog of the WebGL screenshot loop.)

## TRACK D — Modern atmosphere (Round-2 lead "push the Modern look further") ✅ SHIPPED + verified
`chunks/out/M3D_ATMOSPHERE.js`: (A) **weather + day-phase lighting** — `G.battle.wx` (clear/hot/rain/fog/snow) + optional `bd.tod` (dawn/day/dusk/night) drive sun color+intensity, sky color, fog density, hemisphere fill via `_m3dApplyAtmosphere` (HDRI-safe: leaves background to the env if one loaded, always tunes fog). (B) **3D objective flags** — staff + banner over each `M.objs` hex, cloth recolored by `o.owner` (US blue / CS red / neutral grey) each sync, so objective control reads in 3D. Hooked via 3 guarded `typeof` calls added to the parity `_m3dSync` (NOT a re-override — the new chunk only DEFINES the hook fns). VERIFIED in pixels: `modern-weather-fog.png` washes the field into grey-white haze with dim light vs the warm-bright `modern-antietam.png` (clear) — dramatic, correct per-weather mood; objective banners build clean. Full parse PASS, hex 0, `_m3dSync` still 2 defs (atmosphere added calls, not a 3rd def). Classic untouched. NOTE: the parity chunk's spliced `_m3dSync` in the HTML gained the 3 hook lines; the `chunks/out/M3D_PARITY.js` source file mirrors this. Queued next under this track: smoke banks, animated billboard poses, rain/snow particles.

## TRACK 1 — T1 "War Department" systems (1864 Clock / Muster Roll / War Room) ✅ SHIPPED + verified
One cohesive **War Department** strategic shell (Aaron locked 2026-06-14: Fable designs on best judgment, corrects after). Three namespaced append-only chunks (`clk`/`mr`/`wr`, each exposing Init/OnResolve/RenderHTML/Wire) + Fable-authored glue (`chunks/out/T1_SHELL.js`: `openWarDept` tabbed sheet + `_t1Resolve`/`_t1InitAll` hooks + `_wdRefresh`). State lives under `G.campaign.{clock,muster,warroom}` → rides saves free, defensively initialized for old saves, `_SAVE_VER` NOT bumped. Integration = 3 small guarded core edits (campaignAdvance tick, startCampaign init, **newspaper menu** entry "THE WAR DEPARTMENT CONVENES").

**Design choices (Fable's v1 judgment — Aaron, correct anything here):**
- **1864 Clock:** weariness/political-capital/foreign-intervention meters; per-battle deltas (win −6 wear/+10 cap, decisive/objwin bigger; +casualty pressure; intervention asymmetric — CS wins court Europe, US wins cool it). The 1864 referendum is a **recorded verdict, NOT game-over** (support = 100−weariness + cap/2 + winrate·20 ≥ 60 → sustained). War-Bond Drive spends capital → +150 funds (escalating cost).
- **Muster Roll:** permanent ledger of every regiment + fate; auto-names unnamed regiments with period names (e.g. "14th Ohio Infantry"); records battles/credited-kills, marks fallen with where they fell. Read-only v1.
- **War Room:** 5 buildable nodes (side-labeled US Factory/Arsenal/Farm/Railroad/Depot vs CS Tredegar/Niter Bureau/Plantation/...); spend funds → economy output (funds + supply drift + a political-capital trickle into the Clock — the interlink); raider events cut the line. **Guardrail (deliberate): v1 War Room is CAMPAIGN-LAYER only — funds/supply/capital, NOT in-battle combat numbers** (avoids battle-engine regression). Course-correct candidate: make supply feed a small in-battle ammo/morale edge later.

**Audit trail (trust-nothing discipline paid off):** my own read passed all three; the workflow's adversarial auditor caught **2 real `mr` bugs I'd missed**, both verified against live engine before fixing: (1) unnamed regiments' generated period name was clobbered by the engine's generic in-battle label — gate on `u.vetName` (player-supplied) not `u.name` (engine line 953 confirms); (2) `u.kills` is **per-battle** (roster carries no kills field, lines 2655-2661) so `Math.max` undercounts — accumulate instead. Both fixed (<15 lines, patched in place per AUDIT-PROTOCOL).

**Gates:** parse PASS; no invalid hex; no duplicate defs (each fn = 1); functional probe (`tools/t1probe.mjs`) drove a real 3-battle campaign — all 16 fns present, init/tick math correct, **1864 election fires**, both mr fixes confirmed live (name "1st Maine Infantry" preserved, kills 2+1=3 accumulated), War Room build/spend + bond/spend Wire paths work, capital trickle interlink works, **zero errors/pageerrors**. Visual: caught + fixed a real dark-on-dark contrast bug (War Room panel had no bg) — all 3 tabs now parchment "map-room paper", legible + cohesive (`tools/shots/t1-{clock,muster,warroom}.png`). Menu entry reachable + opens (`tools/menuprobe.mjs`, `t1-menu.png`). **Classic + Modern battle regression clean** (antietam/gettysburg re-shot). NOTE: the older shadowed `openMainMenu` (CHUNK-08, line ~3245) carries an inert `mmWarDept` edit — dead code (G6's newspaper `openMainMenu` wins); left as a harmless fallback.

## THE UNLOCK — Fable can now SEE the WebGL renderer

One command (`node tools/shot.mjs [scene…]`) re-shoots any named scene in `tools/shots.json` → real visual regression. This is both Phase 0's eyes-on mechanism AND its stretch goal. `playwright-core` added as a **dev** dep (not loaded at runtime).

**Phase 1 — Modern 3D baseline tuned** (engine core, modern-only `_m3d*`; Classic untouched):

Drop a file in → it lights up, no code change. (The ~7× `404` at battle start is the *expected* one-time probe; no `pageerror`.)
